Current Affairs Commentary

A Word to the Members of the Economic Inspection Delegation to Japan

—Year

Yesterday, this newspaper carried a Central News Agency dispatch that more than a dozen leaders from all sectors of this city were invited by the Japanese side to form an economic inspection delegation, scheduled to depart on the 25th. Since the high tide of economic cooperation between China and Japan, this is a noteworthy event. As far as this reporter knows, since the end of the military confrontation between China and Japan, the activities of the Japanese in contacting and inviting cultural and economic figures from our country to go to Japan for inspection have lasted for many years, and now this economic inspection delegation has finally been realized. This is because, by today, the situation has developed to the point where the Chinese economic circles themselves also need to go to Japan for inspection in order to find ways to overcome the current economic difficulties. This is no longer just accepting an invitation. China has been mired in an unprecedented economic panic in recent years. In order to find a solution, it is necessary to examine the effective methods that various countries have implemented as a reference for formulating a self-rescue plan. The rationale is very clear and does not need detailed explanation. Japan has struggled hard in the world economic panic, and its achievements are seen by the world. There is a reason why it has been able to achieve this. Therefore, it is of great significance for leaders from all sectors to go to inspect and study it. Moreover, the liaison between the authorities of China and Japan on economic cooperation has reached a considerable degree. How the actual implementation will benefit or harm in the future requires sufficient preparation in advance. This trip to the East, on the one hand, is to observe the true intention of the Japanese economic circles regarding the so-called cooperation, and on the other hand, to make an earnest expression of the methods of cooperation that China can accept. This is also an important matter. Since this reporter believes that this trip to the East by leaders from all sectors cannot be compared to an ordinary inspection, I would like to briefly present my views below:

(1) Yesterday's newspaper only listed the names of the leaders from all sectors preparing to go to the East, but the details of the organization of the inspection delegation were missing. This reporter believes that if the inspection delegation wants to make the trip worthwhile, it is necessary to gather assistants with specialized knowledge and experience to accompany them. The inspection should be able to observe subtle details. The leaders' visits and interviews can only cover the general situation. The subtle points of good methods and beautiful intentions cannot be thoroughly understood without a small group of research and practical experience. In order to avoid the criticism of "seeing the flowers from horseback", it is necessary to pay attention to the careful selection of assistants. This concerns the internal organization of the inspection delegation.

(2) There are endless clues to economic inspection. Yesterday's newspaper stated that the nature of this inspection delegation is similar to the previous American economic inspection delegation to China. This reporter has something to say. The American inspection delegation's visit to China was only to understand the trend of China's economic difficulties and to produce a detailed report for the US government's reference for its policy towards China. If China needs to go to Japan for inspection, then what it requires should naturally be more than this. What are the most important points of Japan's economic development? What can be learned from Japan's economic policy to solve China's economic problems? How do Japanese capitalists plan to carry out the so-called economic cooperation between China and Japan? All of this requires a clear understanding in order to fulfill the mission of this inspection. There are still more than two weeks before the departure date, and the leaders have plenty of time to prepare an inspection plan.

Finally, what I want to say is that the trip to the East by leaders from all sectors has the relationship of connecting the economic circles of China and Japan. In this emotional connection, how to inform the Japanese economic circles that the patience of the Chinese people has reached its lowest limit, so as to help realistically adjust the relationship between China and Japan, is also something that needs to be planned in advance. This is another mission that should be had in addition to economic inspection.

New Measures for Reorganizing Mineral Product Tax Newly Drafted by the Ministry of Finance

(Nanjing) To reorganize mineral product tax, the Ministry of Finance newly drafted two measures: (1) Regarding the current collection of mineral products, except for Hubei, Jiangxi, and the coal mines of Dongzhong Xinglu Da, Henan Zhongfu Liuhegou, Anhui Datong Yufan, Zhejiang Changxing, which are managed by special commissioners, and Jiangsu and Hebei, which are temporarily handled concurrently by the unified tax authorities, the remaining provinces have not yet sent personnel to collect the tax. It is planned to first send personnel to prepare for the collection in provinces with abundant mineral products and higher tax revenue, and then extend it to other provinces. (2) In remote areas, due to special circumstances, it is indeed not possible to send personnel to collect taxes for the time being. The Mineral Product Tax Collection Regulations should be consulted, and it should be stipulated that when the mineral products of each province are transported to the provinces that have already started collecting mineral product tax, the first unified tax authority or customs should collect the supplementary tax on behalf of them, so that the national mineral products can be paid equally under the same tax system. (Special dispatch on the 6th)

Beijing's Tax Revenue is Gradually Increasing

(Nanjing) Beijing's tax revenue is gradually increasing. The municipal government has been operating the slaughter tax on its own for a year, with a total revenue of 73,264 yuan. The business tax revenue in the spring was more than 59,000 yuan, and in the summer it was more than 65,000 yuan. (Special dispatch on the 6th)

Brooke Returns to Beijing to Organize All Survey Materials

(Nanjing) Kim University professor and American economic inspector Brooke Louis returned to Beijing on the morning of the 6th to organize all the survey materials. He will send them to the US Department of the Treasury's General Counsel Sothor for transmission to President Roosevelt in a few days. The two men also have personal opinions on improving our country's economic and monetary system, and they have contributed them to our government. It has not yet been decided whether to return to the United States. (Special dispatch on the 6th)

The Ministry of Finance Announces Provisional Measures for Taxing Soda Water

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance announced on the 6th the provisional measures for taxing soda water, with a total of nine articles. Before the promulgation and implementation of the soda water unified tax collection regulations, all domestically produced and imported soda water should be handled in accordance with these measures. Imported soda water will be taxed at 2 cents per pound bottle and 1 cent per half-pound bottle. Domestically produced soda water will be taxed at 1 cent per pound bottle and 5 li per half-pound bottle. The tax will be temporarily collected by the various stamp, tobacco, and liquor tax bureaus. (Central News Agency telegram on the 6th)

Hubei Natives in Beijing Raise Funds for Disaster Relief

(Nanjing) Hubei natives in Beijing have begun to raise funds for disaster relief in their hometowns. Ju Zheng donated 800 yuan alone, and Wang Shijie and Shi Ying each donated 600 yuan. More than 2,000 yuan has been received and sent to the Central Bank on the 6th for remittance to Wuhan for disaster relief. (Central News Agency telegram on the 6th)

Lianyun City Foot Binding Release and Hair Cutting Movement

Starting from the 1st, a two-month period was set for voluntary foot binding release and queue cutting, with mandatory enforcement after the deadline. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Ministry of Justice Issues "Notes on Handling Criminal Litigation Cases"

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Justice, considering that the newly promulgated Criminal Procedure Law is most prone to oversights or misunderstandings, and based on the corrections made by the ministry and court, has compiled one hundred "Notes on Handling Criminal Litigation Cases," detailing matters that should be noted during trials and prosecutions. These have been issued to courts in various provinces for guidance. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Mr. and Mrs. Kong Donate Funds to Relieve Shandong Disaster

(Nanjing) During Kong Xiangxi's recent inspection of the Yellow River disaster, authorities in Jiangsu, Shandong, and along the Jinpu Railway, as well as Sun Tongxuan and others, provided warm hospitality. After arriving in Nanjing, Kong sent telegrams of thanks and, deeply concerned about the famine in Shandong, he and his wife donated 10,000 yuan for disaster relief. A telegram has been sent to Han Fuqu, asking him to allocate the funds on their behalf. The telegram stated, "On the 4th, I personally witnessed the plight of disaster-stricken refugees in Jining, which deeply moved me. My wife and I are donating 10,000 yuan, with 5,000 yuan to be distributed to the disaster victims I saw on the 4th to help them purchase clothes and medicine. Please send personnel to distribute the funds equally to express our sympathy. The remaining amount should be allocated to Shandong disaster relief agencies to assist in the relief efforts for disaster victims throughout the province." It is reported that the funds have been transferred to Han by the Jinan branch of the Central Bank. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Legislators Zhang Weihan and Shi Weihuan Return to Nanjing

(Nanjing) Legislator Zhang Weihan returned to Nanjing on the evening of the 5th after completing his inspection in Yunnan. On the morning of the 6th, he visited Sun Ke at the Legislative Yuan to report on his inspection. He said that he was ordered by Sun to inspect the local self-government facilities in Yunnan. The self-government in Yunnan has been quite successful. The provincial and county councils have been set up, the self-government funds have also been determined, the Baojia in each county has been compiled, and the warehouses have been enriched. The provincial authorities are actively carrying out the establishment of various industries, such as spinning and weaving, hardware factories, cement factories, and refined tin factories. There are no bandits in the province, and the people are living in peace and working happily. In terms of production, Yunnan follows the will of the central government regarding the delimitation of the Yunnan-Burma border. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

(Nanjing) Shi Weihuan, convener of the Labor Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan, returned to Nanjing after completing his inspection of labor conditions in various regions. On the 6th, he told reporters that North China has a foundation in industry, but it is in danger, especially in the spinning, flour, and match factories. Only the carpet and sporting goods businesses are doing better. The reasons are: (1) dumping of foreign goods; (2) decline of the rural economy and weak purchasing power; (3) foreign businesses have better tax treatment than Chinese businesses, making it difficult to compete on price; (4) low production and sales in the industry itself; (5) high transportation costs; (6) increased wages but no increase in work efficiency; and (7) poor factory organization and ineffective management. In addition, the Factory Law is not being implemented in various factories. He will ask the relevant ministry to instruct factory inspectors to pay special attention. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Judicial Yuan Clarifies Penalties for Negligent Acts by Journalists

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan has responded to the request from the Nanjing Journalists' Association to amend the Publication Law and the Criminal Law regarding penalties for negligent acts by journalists, seeking a clear interpretation to ensure their professional safety. The reply from the Judicial Yuan is as follows: Except for the amended Publication Law, which has not yet been promulgated, Article 310 of the Criminal Law regarding defamation does not have special provisions for punishing negligent acts. According to Article 12 of the same law, it only applies to intentional acts. As for the Judicial Yuan's Interpretation No. 303, the so-called "subsequent correction does not affect the establishment of the crime" also refers to intentional acts. The present request is based on a misunderstanding. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Central Museum Architectural Committee Reviews Designs

(Nanjing) The Architectural Committee of the Central Museum held a meeting on the afternoon of the 6th to review architectural designs. Weng Wenhao, Zhang Daofan, and five others attended. Hailstorms in Southern Hebei Damage Crops

(Tianjin) The weather in southern Hebei is abnormal, and the climate is suddenly cold. Hailstorms have occurred in more than ten counties, including Jiahe, Yongnian, Tangxian, Chengan, Gaoyi, and Balongping, destroying half of the autumn crops before they could be harvested. The disaster is particularly severe in Longping, where hail accumulated to half a foot deep on the ground. (Special dispatch, 6th)

(Chongqing) China National Aviation Corporation is actively preparing for the Chengdu-Xikang air route. New-style giant aircraft have been ordered from the United States and will be test-flown upon arrival. Because the terrain is mountainous and the weather changes rapidly, the Chengdu-Ya'an route will be opened first, then extended to Luding in the first step, Kangding in the second step, and Batang in the third step. Once this route is completed, it will be extended from Batang to Qamdo and from Qamdo to Lhasa, completing the Sichuan-Tibet air route. (Central News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Abyssinian Representative Eloquently Defends: Italian Representative Quietly Leaves the Session; Ashamed to be Seated with Abyssinia; Future of League of Nations Mediation Looks Ominous Again

(Geneva) When the League of Nations Administrative Council met tonight, the Italian representative, hearing the Abyssinian representative's remarks, quietly left the meeting place, filled with indignation. The slight hope for a peaceful resolution of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute has now turned for the worse. The meeting was originally scheduled to be held at 6:00 PM tonight, but it was delayed until 7:10 PM when the chairman, Ginazzo, announced the opening of the meeting. Italian Chief Representative Aloisi immediately declared to the audience that he did not want to hear the remarks of Abyssinian Representative Professor Jiji, so when Jiji began to speak, Aloisi withdrew, and Logatelli of the Italian Ministry of Foreign Affairs took his place. Jiji then spoke eloquently, defending Abyssinia. His words were very intense. In the middle of his speech, Logatelli rose and left the case table. Luo left without making a sound. The audience did not notice it until a few minutes later, and then a great disturbance arose. The representatives all felt that this fact was an ominous sign for the future. However, Luo's departure from the meeting place cannot, of course, be interpreted as Italy's withdrawal from the League of Nations.

After Logatelli withdrew, he spoke privately with the chairman, asking him to order Jiji not to make random remarks. Ginazzo replied that he thought there was no reason to stop him, but Soviet Representative Litvinov was about to speak, so he wanted Logatelli to return to the meeting place. Logatelli said that he had to consult the chief representative and asked if the meeting could be suspended for a moment. Ginazzo replied that he could not do this, so Logatelli conveyed Aloisi's opinion, saying that the chief representative must first read the full text of Jiji's speech before he could make a decision. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Abyssinia Invokes Article Fifteen of the Covenant

In his speech, Jiji questioned why Italy wanted to civilize Abyssinia. "Is it reasonable to conscript 100,000 people from a peaceful and happy people and form an army to realize Italy's imperial ambitions? Abyssinia's understanding of civilization is certainly not the creation of a police state for young people." Jiji then invoked Article 10 of the League of Nations Covenant, at which time Logatelli left the meeting place. Jiji continued, "The first step now should be to implement Article 15 of the Covenant to resolve the dispute between the two sides. Do not delay any longer, because further delay will only give Italy the opportunity to prepare for war and defeat the League of Nations with accomplished facts. The Administrative Council has put forward satisfactory suggestions. If Italy accepts it, the disaster of war can be avoided." Jiji then exposed Italy's major conspiracy, saying that its ambition is to disregard everything it wants to destroy. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Italian Representative Leaves the Meeting in a Huff

(Geneva) When the representative of the Abyssinian government gave a speech in the Administrative Council tonight, the Italian representative left the meeting. The League of Nations is quite disturbed by this move. This attitude of the Italian representative is almost inevitable, because yesterday Aloisi said in his speech to the Administrative Council, "If Italy continues to sit at the same table with Abyssinia within the League of Nations with equal qualifications, it cannot help but feel deeply humiliated as a civilized country." It is also unknown whether the Italian representative left in a huff because he heard Professor Jiji's speech, which involved Fascist politics. In this situation, if Italy is not given spiritual satisfaction, Italy may not want to attend meetings again. If Italy is given spiritual satisfaction, most representatives of the Administrative Council believe that it contradicts the principle of freedom of debate in the League of Nations and the sovereignty of member states, which may be difficult to do. Therefore, people are generally deeply afraid that Italy may break with Geneva, or at least break with Geneva on the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. Tonight, French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval is again talking with Polish Foreign Minister Beck, Spanish Representative Madariaga, and Italian Representative Aloisi. The French delegation still hopes that the incident that occurred tonight can be resolved peacefully. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

From the audience's perspective, it was felt that today's speech by Jiji went beyond the scope of diplomatic rhetoric, and it was unnecessary to anger the Italian representative. Now, unless the personal disputes between the Italian and Abyssinian representatives are adjusted, the atmosphere of reconciliation will be difficult to restore for a while. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

(Geneva) It is the intention of people here that Italy may object to French lawyer Professor Jiji continuing to serve as Abyssinia's chief representative. Italian sources said that Logatelli's words in the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting last night were particularly unbearable to hear. If the speaker were an Abyssinian, the situation might be forgivable, but even if he were an Abyssinian, he would have to be more moderate. This can be seen from the remarks made by Abyssinian Ambassador to Paris Hawalit at the last Administrative Council meeting. Jiji's remarks are unbearable, and although the Italian representative wanted to leave to the end, he was unable to do so. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

Litvinov Speaks Uprightly for Justice

Following Jiji, the speaker was Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov. Litvinov officially said that the relationship between the Soviet Union and Italy has been very harmonious in the past ten years, and he hopes that this friendship will continue. However, he cannot support Italy's proposal that the League of Nations not question the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. Italy has not denied attacking Abyssinia. This attack is tantamount to tearing up the League of Nations Covenant and creating a bad example for the future. Fortunately, the principle of peace is indivisible is gradually gaining the people's belief. He finds it difficult to acknowledge that violence can be resorted to simply because of the internal affairs of a country. As the Italian memorandum said, no one has expressed sympathy for the current situation in Abyssinia, but it cannot be discriminated against simply because of the different skin color and backward culture of a country. All countries enjoy the right to independence and to maintain territorial integrity, but there is no excuse for using force except for self-defense. Litvinov finally proposed the Kellogg-Briand Pact, asking the League of Nations to take risks to save the disaster of war. There were no subsequent speeches (National News dispatch, 5th)

At this point, the chairman, Argentine Representative Guazú, expressed the hope that a procedure for resolving the Italian-Abyssinian dispute could be presented at the next meeting. The Administrative Council then announced the adjournment of the meeting, which was at 8:20 PM. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Agreement Reached to Form a Five-Nation Committee

(Geneva) New difficulties have now arisen regarding the organization of a special committee to investigate the Italian-Abyssinian dispute in accordance with Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant. Because Britain and France are related parties, Italy opposes their joining, and small countries are unwilling to bear the heavy responsibility of the committee. Spain, Turkey, and Poland had previously said they were willing to join the committee, but now they have stated that if Britain and France do not join because of Italy's opposition, they will reconsider their previous proposal. However, Italy firmly maintains that if British and French representatives join the committee, Italy must also join, and that Italy does not oppose any committee appointed by the League of Nations, nor does it apply to join any committee. British Representative Eden and French Prime Minister Laval met this morning. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol and the representatives of Poland, Spain, and Turkey all came to meet. Although they had a long closed-door meeting, it is said that they dispersed without any results. Italian Representative Aloisi then visited Avenol to formally protest the remarks made by Abyssinian Representative Professor Jiji yesterday, but the Italian side denied that Aloisi had asked that Jiji not be recognized as a Ming representative. It is said that Professor Jiji is unwilling to apologize to the Italian representative, nor is he willing to change his rhetoric. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

(Geneva) After holding meetings one after another today, an agreement was finally reached in the evening to organize a special committee composed of representatives from Britain, France, Poland, Spain, and Turkey to handle the Italian-Abyssinian dispute in accordance with Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

The Emperor's Imperial Guard numbers approximately 40,000, all trained by European officers. The Archbishop and government officials will also accompany the Emperor. Furthermore, 100,000 well-trained volunteers will serve as the two wings of the Emperor's Imperial Guard and provide rear guard protection. Before the end of the rainy season, if war breaks out with the Italian army, mules and horses will be temporarily used. Once the land dries out, fifty transport vehicles will be used to transport the Emperor's Imperial Guard. It is heard that the Emperor's Bodyguard will support the fiercest aspects of the war. French Shooting Expert Appointed to Important Air Force Post

(Paris) - During the European War, French Air Force officer Georges Guynemer, renowned for his marksmanship, was considered the strongest of the strong in the Air Force. After the European War, he turned to political life and was elected as a member of the Chamber of Deputies. Having been away from military service for eighteen years, he was suddenly summoned by Minister of Aviation General Victor Denain and given an important mission: to research and improve aerial shooting methods. During the European War, Guynemer would often fly his plane alone into German lines, shooting down multiple enemy aircraft with only a few bullets. He often shot down an airplane with only a few bullets, so he was invincible and often did not use much ammunition. Guynemer also had an exceptional skill, being able to shoot a five-franc silver coin (about the size of a Chinese silver dollar) at fifty meters with a pistol. General Denain summoned Guynemer because of his excellent shooting skills. Currently, there are two schools of thought in the air forces of various countries regarding the issue of shooting: one advocates the use of high-speed cannons, while the other favors the use of machine guns. These two schools of thought are also in dispute within the French Air Force. Guynemer will now serve as an arbiter. He will personally go to the shooting school in Cazaux and conduct experiments with the latest aircraft, which can reach speeds of over 400 kilometers per hour, and will study pilot training methods. (Sixth Havas Telegram)

Germany's Trade with China Shows Surplus; Chinese Egg Exports to Germany Increase Sharply This Year

(Berlin) - Germany's trade with China in the first half of this year showed a surplus. From January to June this year, Germany's exports to China reached 47.7 million marks, an increase of 9.9 million marks compared to the first half of 1934. However, this is still 10 million marks less than the total value of Chinese goods imported into Germany. In the first half of this year, China's exports to Germany were 57 million marks, while in the first half of 1934, they were 64.4 million marks. According to economic observers, the reason for the increase in German exports to China is due to the purchase of a large batch of railway materials after the conclusion of the Chinese railway purchase contract. However, there has been a decreasing trend in other German goods exported to China. For example, in the first half of 1934, Germany's artificial silk exports to China were approximately 900,000 marks, while in the first half of this year, they were only 600,000 marks. In the first half of this year, the quantity of Chinese eggs imported into Germany increased. German stationery, automobile bicycle, paint, and perfume imports into China decreased significantly. However, Chinese-made coarse yarn exports to Germany increased threefold. Chinese sheepskin production also increased. Chinese wool imports into Germany doubled, while cotton increased fourfold. (Fifth Havas Telegram)

US Continues to Purchase Silver to Reach the Ratio of Gold to Silver of 3:1

(Washington) - Senator Thomas, leader of the silver faction in the Senate, stated today that when Congress reopens next January, the white silver, rural, and pension gold triple faction members will work together to seek currency inflation. At the same time, Treasury Secretary Henry Morgenthau Jr. also stated that the Treasury Department intends to give the Pittman Committee all the reference it should have. It is generally believed that the Treasury Department does not intend to disclose to the committee the details of the use of the 200 million yuan stabilization fund. The Treasury Secretary once said that, according to the law, the Treasury Department has no obligation to provide Congress with any information about the fund before next spring. According to the figures released by the Treasury Department today, the United States has purchased 500 million ounces of silver since the implementation of the Silver Purchase Act. The current silver holdings of the National Army have reached 1,159,000,000 ounces, valued at US$1,485,000,000. If it is to achieve the ratio of gold to silver of 3:1, it is still necessary to purchase 1.3 billion ounces. If the price of silver can reach $1.29 soon, it will not be necessary to purchase enough. Thomas said today that he is eager to see the report of the stabilization fund, but he feels that the Treasury Secretary has failed to prepare an explanation of the provision in the Silver Purchase Act that authorizes the government to issue silver certificates, so the Treasury Department's actions are not in line with the original intention of Congress. After the silver is purchased, it is not issued as currency at a price of $1.19 or the purchase price to make it circulate, so there will be action when Congress reopens. (Fifth National Telegram)

Roosevelt Indicates That the New Deal Can Be Suspended; Basic Procedures Are Mostly Completed; Response to a Letter from Roy Howard

(New York) - Roy Howard, the owner of a famous newspaper, once told President Roosevelt that businessmen are alarmed and fear that there is no hope for national recovery unless the government's experimental behavior is stopped. Today, President Roosevelt replied in a letter, saying that the current government had undertaken a large-scale legislative procedure before taking office, but the basic procedure has almost been completed and can be rested for a while. This statement by President Roosevelt can be considered very important because it indicates that there may not be any major legislation before the presidential election next year at the earliest, and the fact that President Roosevelt is willing to allow businessmen to adopt their own ways to seek recovery can also be learned from this. (Sixth Reuters Telegram)

A Record of Inspecting the Disaster Situation of Rivers and Canals: The Disaster Situation of the Dongzhuang Breach and Its Trends

— Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Geng

Going east from Huangzhuang for over ten li to Liuzhuang is the first dangerous section on the south bank of the Yellow River in Hebei Province. Baskets of bricks and straw are piled up like bunkers. The sound of the strong currents rushing against the dikes and dams is startling. The river workers in that section are working hard to protect it, and so far, there have been no accidents, which is admirable. Traveling northeast along the dike for over twenty li, we entered the territory of Heze County in Shandong Province. There were many disaster victims on the dike, each holding a stalk of sorghum. They had nothing else of value. Hunchbacked, they carried their children, as if they were fleeing to other places. When they saw strangers, or those in cars, they would cry out for help in unison. Those who sought refuge in straw shacks were even more likely to gather in groups and surround visitors, begging for relief. Women with bound feet and braided hair would reach out with the crowd, but immediately retreat shyly behind others. Their situation was very pitiful. Along the way, we repeatedly saw makeshift sedan chairs made of door panels and willow branches, carrying brides. There were no flags, drums, or dowries. Only a piece of red cloth was occasionally hung on the sedan chair. In this situation, the bride's family has already been scattered and displaced due to the disaster, so they are hastily sending her to her husband's family. The groom's family is also mostly living outdoors, unable to take care of themselves. They have no strength to welcome her, but they cannot refuse her either, so they have to reluctantly accept and complete the wedding. Although marriage is called a comedy, in the disaster area, both the bride's and groom's families see the bride as a burden. It is truly a reflection of tragedy.

This time, the Dongzhuang breach has caused six townships and four hundred villages in northern Heze to be completely submerged. The disaster is severe, far exceeding that of 1933 tenfold. The number of people who have drowned, starved to death, or died from epidemics is countless. Those who have not died are mostly temporarily taking refuge on rooftops, treetops, dikes, or hills, without support or food, living day to day. Although they have not died yet, they are already living next to death. The situation is tragic and urgent, and they are all eagerly awaiting rescue. Chen Yasan, the county magistrate of Heze, and Qin Jianbin, Peng Zhanyuan, Zhang Yingzhu, and others, have organized disaster relief centers, using old temples or building straw sheds. All disaster victims, regardless of county boundaries, are accepted. As of mid-August, a total of 25,560 disaster victims have been accommodated in 94 relief centers, managed by 16 branches. However, the disaster victims who have been accommodated only account for one-tenth or two-tenths of all the disaster victims in the county. In addition, there are 200,000 disaster victims who are struggling daily in the wind and rain. Although various charitable organizations have made some donations and the government has also allocated funds, the disaster area is very large and there are extremely many disaster victims, so the distribution is limited, and it is ultimately a drop in the bucket.

The river dike in Heze County is 40 li long and extends northeast into Juancheng County. Soon, it reaches Dongzhuang. The great embankment, the people's dike, and the Jiangsu dam are lined with mud houses and straw sheds, all temporary residences for disaster victims. The old houses on the plain south of the dike are close to the breach. Initially, they were flooded by the Yellow River. Then, because the breach opened in six places, the strong currents shifted eastward, and the old houses were silted up with mud and sand to a depth of five or six feet. Some only have their doors and windows half-exposed, while others only have the roofs visible. It is impossible to crawl in, and it is clear how cramped their living conditions are. Walking from the Jiangsu dam to the riverbank, the massive current is turbulent and extremely frightening. The river mud is swirled by the backflow, and a cracking sound is faintly heard. Then, huge chunks collapse into the river. This is the so-called "autumn river digging the bottom," which is extremely harmful. At that time, there was a sailboat about to cross to the opposite bank to observe the water flow of the breach and inquire about the disaster situation in Juancheng. So, we boarded the boat to cross. The river surface is about three li wide. Each crossing takes one hour. Initially, we rowed against the current along the bank, and it was still stable enough to sit. Then, we hoisted the sail and went with the current, and it became shaky and unstable. The strong current was rapid, like ten thousand horses galloping. The waves rose and fell very high. The boat moved up and down with the waves, sometimes rising on the crest, sometimes hidden in the trough. Looking at the willows on the bank, they appeared and disappeared. There were 18 passengers, mostly women and children with pale faces. The boatman told everyone to sit or lie down and not move. Hearing this, my heart jumped uneasily. After crossing the strong current, it was as stable as before. When we arrived at the newly built dam in Juancheng, the police asked and learned that the passengers were disaster victims, and then allowed us to dock and go ashore.

The base of the dam is 12 zhang wide, the top is 3.6 zhang wide, 1.2 zhang high, and over 200 zhang long. It intersects with the people's dike and the great embankment (i.e., the Jin embankment), forming a right-angled triangle. The Yellow River flows diagonally northeast from Dongzhuang, and the people's dike runs parallel to the river like a string. The great embankment also extends east from Dongzhuang like a hook. On July 10th, the Yellow River water rose sharply, overflowing the people's dike at the edge of the string around 2:00 PM. After 6:00 PM, it successively broke through the openings of the great embankment on the sides of the triangle. The officials and people of Juancheng mobilized 20,000 to 30,000 people day and night to rush to complete the dam on the sides of the triangle in two days and nights, so that the flood did not directly hit the urban area of Juancheng, preserving a piece of dry land that accounted for about one-third of the entire territory (the urban area is more than 30 li east of the dam, surrounded by the great embankment and the people's dike). Currently, Qin Daoyu, the county magistrate of the county, Wang Jinghan, the captain of the guard team, and various gentry leaders are all working in the straw sheds on the dam, one to protect the unbroken embankments and the other to plan for post-disaster relief. Many disaster victims from nearby Linpu, Shijia, Baiyi, and other villages that have not been washed away are gathered here. When they saw the reporter coming ashore, some called him "official" and begged for casual relief. The weather was very hot. When we bought watermelon, fearing contamination by flies, we discarded the cut surface. The women and children standing beside us immediately swarmed to eat it, which was unbearable. We selected the sick and administered some medicine. The crowd probably misunderstood that we were providing relief, so they surrounded us. The police worked hard to extricate us, and we were able to escape. Later, we visited the county magistrate and others, who insisted on having lunch with us. The dishes were rich and delicious. When we asked how the disaster area could have such food, someone answered that Chairman Han had come here yesterday and it was specially prepared to entertain him. Later, the disaster victims surrounded him begging for relief, and Chairman Han, unable to bear the disturbance, soon had something to do in Dongzhuang, so he did not return for the banquet. Now, we happened to meet, so we were invited to a banquet. Although we were treated with great kindness and urged to eat, it was difficult to swallow and eat our fill, surrounded by the wailing people outside.

Juancheng is located in the western border of Shandong Province, near the south bank of the Yellow River. This time, the Yellow River suddenly breached in six places at Linpu Village east of Dongzhuang in the county, with a width of over 500 zhang. Currently, the first to fourth breaches have been completely silted up as dry breaches, with silt reaching a depth of eight feet. Linpu Village was originally a large town. Only one lonely temple remains in the entire town, because the construction was high and solid, it was not washed away, and is now still half-buried in the silt. The fifth and sixth breaches have been washed together into one, with a width of over 200 zhang, or more than one li. The Yellow River is flowing out torrentially from here, and it is unknown what harm it will cause. The terrain of the main river is very high, and the terrain outside the breach is low and sloping. Water flows downhill, so only 20% of the water remains in the main river, and the remaining 80% flows out through the breach. South of the official dike, i.e., outside the breach, has not been flooded since the first year of Guangxu's reign. The ground is more than one zhang lower than the beach, so the waves are rolling and flowing like a waterfall. The deep floodwaters are rushing east to more than ten counties in western Shandong, turning everywhere into a vast ocean and a swamp. From Dongzhuang in the west of Juancheng to Wu'an in the east (a village in Yuncheng County), and from the official dike in the north to Shuncheng in the south, over 8,000 qing of land have been submerged, and many people and livestock have drowned. Among the corpses, there were even families of more than ten people tied together with ropes, or tied to the necks of cows, hoping that the cows would float them out of the water, but it was unsuccessful. As for those who climbed trees and squatted on rooftops, boats hired at the flood site had to take two or three days to rescue them because they were going against the current. Many of the elderly were already dying. In total, there are 200,000 disaster victims in the county, over 2,000 drowned, and property losses of over 1.84 million yuan, and 80% to 90% of the land has been silted up, so the losses are impossible to estimate. The county's disaster relief centers are located in nine places, including the county seat, Xinyi Village, and Gulin Temple, accommodating over 30,000 qualified disaster victims. The principle of family cohabitation is adopted. The disaster victims provide their own straw sheds as residences in designated areas. Those who do not have any utensils are given additional subsidies. Each disaster victim is given 1.5 yuan per month for cooking expenses, and they cook their own meals. The able-bodied disaster victims are required to undertake the obligation of repairing roads, guarding embankments, and all public labor services. In addition, disaster victims are divided into three departments: children, adults, and women, each given appropriate education in literacy and vocational skills. The organization is still relatively complete.

The Yellow River breached on July 10th, and almost two months have passed. Although the authorities have repeatedly made agreements to carry out the process of blocking the breach and diverting the Zi River back to the Yellow River, they have not been prepared to implement it. The rolling Yellow River water is pouring southeast, flowing away like that, and it will not wait for me. It has first brought disaster to more than ten counties in western Shandong, including Juancheng, Jining, Yutai, Dongping, Wenshang, Jinxiang, Yuncheng, Heze, Juye, and Jiaxiang, and has filled the major lakes of Shushan, Zhaoyang, and Weishan. It has gone straight to northern Jiangsu and has already flooded the four counties of Feng, Pei, Tong, and Pi. Recently, it has expanded the disaster area along the Central Canal. Even if the breach is blocked now and the source is cut off, it has already become a problem to drain the accumulated water. Moreover, blocking the breach requires a huge sum of 3 million yuan, and transporting and preparing stone materials requires a period of three or four months, which is already a situation of being caught off guard. If it is still allowed to continue flowing, the huge open-air flow cannot be limited to western Shandong and northern Jiangsu, and it will become saturated. Then, it is inevitable that the Yellow River will change its course and enter the sea. Judging from its trend, it is likely to enter the sea through the Central Canal and the Liutang River. The increasingly expanding disaster area is truly unimaginable.

The cause of the disaster is that heavy rain in the upper reaches in early July caused the river flow to increase sharply. The river bottom in the lower reaches is more than one meter higher than last year due to siltation, and the water level has exceeded the records of previous years by between half a meter and one meter. This is a natural disaster. As for the human causes, the Yellow River Conservancy Commission invested 1.5 million yuan for the cost of raising and thickening the great embankments in various provinces. A special appropriation of 100,000 yuan was made for the section from Zhukou to Dongzhuang, with Zhang Lianjia, the Director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau, responsible for it. However, the dike works in Henan and Hebei have all been completed, but the section from Zhukou to Dongzhuang has not been completed, resulting in the accident. When the people's dike was initially overflowing and the great embankment subsequently collapsed, and when the Wang Tan great embankment five li east of the breach was in danger, the people pleaded for rescue, but Zhang Lianjia evaded and refused to go, citing the large water flow and lack of labor and materials. The Wang Tan dangerous work was protected from danger by the people of the urban area, who had a direct interest in life and property, and who did their best to protect it. Other people's dikes assigned to the people for protection have not collapsed, so the disaster victims in various counties are quite dissatisfied with Zhang Lianjia.

Tianjin's Various Economic Organizations Are Established One After Another; The East Asia Tonghui Company Emerges; The East Asia Economic Association Is Formed

Tianjin Communication: Niu Chuanqi, Shen Tongwu, Liu Xiangye, Chen Dingyuan, Chen Zeliang, and others, under the pretext of promoting economic cooperation in East Asia and developing various industries, have formed the East Asia Economic Association. The association has been preparing since the middle of last month, and was officially opened on the 3rd at No. 1 Yongping Lane, Mingli Street, Japanese Concession. Niu Chuanqi, Shen Tongwu, and Liu Xiangye are in charge of everything. It is heard that the purpose is to introduce Japanese capital into the industrial circles of Tianjin, Hebei, and major cities in North China in the name of helping development, and to purchase raw materials produced in China on behalf of Japanese industrial companies. In terms of its nature, it is probably an introducing agency. However, it is also heard that the association is backed by a branch of the newly established Japanese International Banking Company in Tianjin, and all plans are instructed by the company. In addition to this association, Gao Ling and Wang Shuangqi and others have initiated the North China Economic Relief Committee. The proposal to organize the association was made earlier than the East Asia Economic Association, but later, due to the proposal of the Japanese military to set up a staff headquarters and the Xingzhong Company in Tianjin, it was intended to incorporate the association, so the progress was somewhat suspended. Now, Gao Ben Lulang, chairman of the Sino-Japanese Industrial Company for North China Economic Cooperation, believes that the association still needs to be organized independently, and specially promoted the realization of the association. It is also heard that there are many similar organizations, all in the process of brewing.

The Tianjin Chamber of Commerce held a joint meeting of executive and supervisory committees on the 1st of this month, and resolved to organize the East Asia Tonghui Trading Company. It nominated Pan Yansheng (president of Junqian Hospital in the Japanese Concession), Bian Shoujing (former speaker of the Zhili Provincial Assembly), Yu Fuchen (former secretary of the Construction Bureau), Niu Huiqing (recommended by Sakai, staff officer of the Japanese Garrison), Gong Wenqing (professor of the Japanese Garrison), and Liu Yibai, Lu Junyu, Chen Houwen, and Cao Dianqiu as members of the preparatory committee, with Pan Yansheng concurrently serving as director of the preparatory committee. On the afternoon of the 3rd, the first preparatory meeting was held again at the Chamber of Commerce, and Pan Yansheng, Bian Shoujing, and Niu Huiqing were nominated as drafters to draft the organizational charter, establishing an import-export and Japanese goods introduction company in Tianjin for the entire dumping plan. The North China Japanese Garrison fully sponsored it, and the municipal government had not even heard of the proposal beforehand. The association has not been registered with the official authorities, but its organization is very active. (4th)

Songjiang: Verdict on the Case of the Special Committee Member Shooting and Killing a Person

Min Xiaozhang and Chen Zihe, members who handle special affairs, received a report from an informant last month that Zhu Qinbo, who was suspected of something, was to be arrested in Wuzhen. Under the pretext of randomly checking household registration, the suspect was lured out. During the dispute, Committee Member Chen and others shot and killed Zhu Qinbo's father, Fu Zhen. The villagers were indignant and beat the committee members and injured them. They were taken to the county government and transferred to the local court for interrogation. A report was submitted to the superiors, and the two committee members Chen and Min were dismissed. The case has been tried repeatedly and the verdict was announced on the morning of this day. The master of the case briefly stated that the defendant Chen Zihe was sentenced to five years of imprisonment for murder, and Min Xiaozhang was fined 40 yuan for negligent injury. Zhu Qinbo and Zhu Wenshan were fined 15 yuan for illegally depriving people of their freedom. Zhu Xinshan was fined 15 yuan for the part of hurting people. Zhu Shushan and Zhu Deshan were found not guilty. Chen Zihe should compensate Zhu Zhu for 100 yuan for the cost of the coffin. The fines were enforced against each defendant, and those who were unable to pay would be replaced with one day of labor for each yuan. After the judgment was completed, Chen and others were taken back into custody.

Qingpu: The County Government Arrests the Guan Chuan Members

The county government suddenly dispatched a large number of public security teams and the entire class of bailiffs at 11:00 AM yesterday to arrest the Guan Chuan members. As a result, 11 people, including Lu Chunsen, Huai Ansheng, and Zhang Rujun, were arrested. Fifteen people have not been arrested. By 4:00 PM, the residences of Guan Chuan members Yan Bingyong and Wang Zhenhuan were sealed by the county government, and family members were summoned. The remaining arrests are still being carried out strictly. It is heard that the content of the case and the reason for the arrests is that there are a total of 26 Guan Chuan members in this county, and their offices have always been in private residences, which has been the case for many years. Recently, the county government believes that it is inappropriate for the Guan Chuan members to work in private residences. The county magistrate summoned all the Guan Chuan members for a training session on August 29th, saying: 1. Those with pending cases must not serve as Guan Chuan members; 2. Those with concurrent jobs must not serve as Guan Chuan members; 3. Guan Chuan members who are unwilling to comply should immediately declare their resignation and wait for another appointment. Those who do not arrive at the government office by 8:00 AM on the 31st will be deemed to have resigned; 4. Regardless of whether Guan Chuan members are retained or retired, all public property and booklets should be submitted to the county government. They must not leave the government before they are cleared. At that time, each Guan Chuan member said that the public property booklets were all at home, and most of the family members were illiterate, so they certainly could not hand them over one by one. Therefore, Qin Shuqiu, the collection director, and Lu Chunsen, the Guan Chuan director, issued a guarantee, limiting each Guan Chuan member to hand them over to the county government the next day. Each Guan Chuan member did hand them over on time the next day. However, when the deadline of the 31st arrived, each Guan Chuan member believed that working in the county government would reduce work efficiency, so they followed the third point of Magistrate Qian's training and did not come to the government to express their resignation. Magistrate Qian believed that it was a resistance to government orders, so he dispatched a large number of armed public security teams and others to arrest them yesterday (the 4th). When the arrest order was issued, the doors of the collection office and the telephone room were guarded by police, and the situation was unusually tense. The arrested Guan Chuan members were immediately taken to the detention center. Various local agencies, unaware of the truth about the sudden arrest of a large number of Guan Chuan members by the county government, sent representatives to visit the county magistrate to inquire about the truth. The county magistrate, believing that the situation was serious, was inconvenient to explain, and the representatives left without any information.

Suzhou: The Crystal Daily Reporter's Case Opens

The case of Wu County Crystal Daily reporter Wang Zhuxin being sued for defamation by Lu Guanhui, a Suzhou gentleman from Tianguanfang, opened in the local court yesterday morning (the 6th). The plaintiff did not arrive and was represented by lawyer Wu Chao. The defendant Wang Zhuxin arrived at the court with lawyers Zhuang Xiangren and Tian Qiang to respond to the interrogation. After being interrogated by Judge Shen Bingrong, the defendant Wang Zhuxin was released on bail to await a scheduled retrial. The plaintiff's lawyer was instructed that Lu Guanhui should personally attend the next court hearing.

The Highway Bureau Stops the Opening of the Su-Mu Road

After the completion of the Su-Mu section of the Su-Fu Highway, it started operating on the 1st of this month, selling tickets and carrying passengers. The business was still fairly good, but Director Shen of the Provincial Highway Bureau believed that the Su-Mu Road had not yet obtained a business license, so how could it be opened and operated without permission? Yesterday, he specially telegraphed the Wu County Construction Bureau, ordering them to stop the opening of the road in order to comply with the regulations. The Su-Fu Long-Distance Bus Company stated that although it had not yet obtained a business license, it had already obtained a test driving permit from the Construction Bureau, so it submitted a request to the Highway Bureau, stating everything and requesting the issuance of a business license.

Wuxi: Frequent Zhenxin Labor Strikes

The Zhenxin Yarn Factory outside the West Gate experienced a labor strike in mid-July. The factory stated that it was unable to maintain operations due to the high cost of cotton and the low price of yarn, so it stopped work at the end of July. The workers, however, stated that the factory had not paid their wages for June and July, leading to a major strike. After the Party and government, together with the Chamber of Commerce, made great efforts to mediate, two installments of wages were paid on August 5th and 9th, and it was announced that work would resume in one month, and the strike was quelled. Later, Manager Jiang Zheqing went to Shanghai for medical treatment and sent a letter from the board of directors announcing his resignation. Associate Manager Rong Xuxin hid and refused to meet, so no one was responsible. The one-month deadline for resuming work has arrived. Hua Shaocun, the business director, contacted the Party and government and the workers, and it was agreed that work would resume immediately after the new cotton was launched. Before the negotiations could be completed, Manager Jiang Zheqing suddenly telegraphed the staff from Shanghai, telling them to return to their respective homes and wait for notification to return to the factory when a car was available. At the same time, the factory's electric lights were cut off and food was stopped. The staff were greatly panicked, because the factory had not paid the salaries for August, and many of the staff came from Hunan, Jiangxi, and other provinces. Now, it was impossible to stay and impossible to leave. Therefore, more than 40 staff members, including Wang Zhiping, found the director of affairs, Qin Liangcai, and together they petitioned the county Party headquarters and demanded three things from the factory: (1) Pay the salaries for August; (2) If there is no hope of opening the factory, a severance fee must be paid; (3) Staff from other provinces must be given travel expenses. The two committee members Sun and Xu of the Party headquarters instructed them to wait patiently for mediation. The staff then dragged Qin Liangcai back to the factory, vowing to share the joys and sorrows. On the workers' side, because the factory treated the staff like this, all the savings and unpaid wages would definitely be lost. Yesterday, they also went to the Party headquarters in groups to request relief. The factory's disputes are numerous, and it is feared that they cannot be resolved in a short time.

Modification of New Measuring Instruments for the Rice and Bean Industry

The local county government, in order to implement the new system of weights and measures, originally intended to facilitate the daily needs of the people and standardize goods. Since its implementation in this county, all industries in the region have complied and adopted it. Various districts and townships have been repeatedly urged to purchase new instruments and replace the old ones on schedule. However, with the exception of length and weight measures which have been replaced, there are still many who procrastinate and wait when it comes to measuring instruments, and have not yet complied. This has led to discrepancies and confusion in commercial transactions, easily breeding malpractices. In order to strictly enforce uniformity, all grain shops, stores, warehouses, and businesses in the county are required to uniformly use the new system of "sheng" and "dou" measures starting from September 15th of this year. Those who continue to outwardly comply but secretly violate the regulations by privately using the old system, once discovered through inspection, will be severely punished according to Chapter 13 of the criminal law. A public notice was specifically issued yesterday to inform everyone. Regarding the conversion of new and old measuring instruments: 1 dou equals 1 shi, which is approximately equivalent to 9 dou and 3 sheng and 4 he of the tribute grain measure. 1 dou of the tribute grain measure equals 1 shi and 0.07 sheng of the market measure.

Changzhou - Suicide by Hanging Due to Economic Hardship

Fei Rongsheng, a resident outside the North Gate of Wu County, was over 40 years old and worked as a woodworker. His wife and children had passed away in previous years. Recently, due to the lack of work, he was unable to make a living, and developed a pessimistic view of life. Around 7 PM on the 5th, he hanged himself in front of his bed and died. Afterwards, the neighborhood chief, Lü Jinhong, reported it to the Second Public Security Precinct and requested that the local court send personnel to conduct an autopsy.

Jiangyin - Labor Unrest Calmed at Hua Cheng Cloth Factory

Female workers at the Hua Cheng Dyeing and Weaving Second Cloth Factory went on strike on the 2nd due to wage issues. Female worker Xu Er-mei and others were dismissed, and over 20 female workers went on a full strike, petitioning the Party headquarters and demanding that the factory accept two conditions: (1) Dismissed female workers to be reinstated; (2) Restore wages. On the morning of the 4th, Special Commissioner Zhang invited Hua Cheng manager Han Xi'an and Section Chief Ge Shaowu of the county government's First Section to meet and discuss for two hours. By the afternoon, it was decided that the dismissed female workers would be allowed to return to work. As for the issue of restoring wages, a wage standard would be determined after the County Party Headquarters, together with the County Government, sent personnel to the factory to investigate the actual economic situation. The female workers were satisfied and uniformly returned to work on the 5th.

Nantong - New Cotton from Tongzhou, Rugao, and Hai'an Has Entered the Market

Tongzhou, Rugao, and Hai'an counties are prosperous cotton-producing areas. This year, due to favorable weather conditions of sunshine and rain, coupled with autumn heat, the cotton crop is in excellent condition. The harvest season has now arrived. According to estimates by the provincial Langshan Cotton Farm, the output of medium cotton and miscellaneous cotton within the region is approximately 923,000 shi. New cotton from the surrounding villages has entered the market. Cotton merchants from the Jiangnan region are flocking north to set up shops and purchase goods, and the financial market has become lively.

Yuxi Cracks Down on Illegal Opium Trafficking Case

After learning that Zhou Ruzhong's family in Yuxi was selling illegal opium, anti-narcotics investigators went to search the premises. Zhou was out at the time, and his wife and daughter panicked, attempting to pour the opium into a chamber pot. They were intercepted with witnesses and evidence, and were taken to the county government for interrogation.

Haimen - Large Quantity of Illegal Opium Intercepted

Wu Tingfang (also known as "Little Guangdong"), a notorious opium trafficker from Qidong Weijiao Town, transported and sold illegal opium in Haimen and Qidong counties in large quantities, profiting handsomely. The day before yesterday afternoon, he had 16 packages of illegal opium, weighing a total of 228 taels and worth over 600 yuan, transported from Shanghai, hidden in the bottom of a shoe basket, and delivered to his home by rickshaw puller Chen Xilin. Unexpectedly, the information was leaked, and someone secretly reported it to the County Anti-Narcotics Association. The police were dispatched and intercepted the rickshaw puller in Nanshi, Weijiao Town, and brought him and the illicit goods to the association for investigation. Wu Tingfang fled upon hearing the news and could not be captured.

Pinghu - Murdered Female Corpse Found in City River

On the evening of the 4th, a floating corpse was discovered in the city river in front of the Chenghuang Temple. The local bailiff reported it to the authorities, who requested an autopsy. Coroner Du Cheng took the coroner to the scene and determined that the corpse was that of a woman, around twenty years old. Her mouth was open, her tongue was curled up, her abdomen had been cut open with a knife, her intestines were protruding, and one foot had rotted and the skin had peeled off. It was clearly a case of murder followed by disposal of the body in the water. One theory is that the corpse floated from Jiaxing. Because it was the spring tide that day, the currents were extremely swift, and the corpse floated through the city and into the East Lake area, stopping in front of the Chenghuang Temple due to the river embankment. The corpse has been placed in a coffin and temporarily buried in the public cemetery pending investigation.

Ningbo - Red Pill Female Trafficker Executed by Firing Squad

Dong Zhangshi, a widow from Shipu Shuimentou in Xiangshan, operated a small store in name but sold red pills in reality. In April, when Hu Quanhu was buying red pills from Dong Zhangshi, he was apprehended on the spot by police officers from the Second Public Security Precinct. The evidence and illicit goods were transferred to the county government for investigation. The suspect confessed to the trafficking without denial and was sentenced to death according to the law. The case file was submitted to the commissioner's office and then to the military headquarters for review. Subsequently, Execution Order No. 4399 and Commissioner's Office Order No. 1368 were received, approving the execution. The suspect was taken out yesterday morning at 7 AM, her identity was confirmed, and she was escorted to the West Parade Ground for execution by firing squad.

Passenger on Ningxing Steamer Jumps into the Sea

On the previous day, a male passenger in his twenties with a Suzhou accent, traveling on the Sanbei Company's Ningxing steamer from Shanghai to Ningbo, occupied a berth on the starboard side of the third deck. He had no luggage. After the ship sailed out of the Wusong Estuary, the passenger suddenly jumped off the deck into the sea. Upon receiving the report, the captain turned the ship around, but there was no way to rescue him. Afterwards, the ship's crew found a diary in his berth with three letters written in pencil: one to his parents, one to his wife, and one to his wife's younger brother and sister-in-law. On the back page of the diary, the phrase "A happy couple / A hateful enemy" was written, followed by the name "Jiemei" and an English signature. The phonetic transcription of the name was Tao Jiemei. Because the first page of his diary contained the words "Respectfully requesting that this photo be reproduced in the newspaper so that my family in Wu County may understand my fate, I would be eternally grateful," it was clear that the deceased was a resident of Suzhou named Tao Jiemei. As there was no address for the ship's crew to send the items to, they had to keep all of his belongings for safekeeping.

Mingguang - Bandits Rob Merchants at Huayuanzui

Ding Denian, a grain merchant from this port, along with his companions Chen and others, carried over 1,500 yuan and traveled by boat to buy grain outside the river. Unexpectedly, last night when the boat arrived at Huayuanzui, over a dozen bandits dressed in uniforms and speaking with a Haizhou accent suddenly boarded the ship with guns, claiming to be conducting an inspection. They robbed Ding and his companions of all their money. Ding, sensing danger, escaped in the chaos. The whereabouts of Chen and the others are unknown.

Commemoration Measures

(2) Date: September 9th, 9:00 AM.

(3) Venue: Municipal Party Committee Auditorium.

(4) Chairman of the Assembly: to be assumed by a member of the Municipal Party Committee.

(5) Starting September 8th, publish a notice in the newspaper for two days, informing all municipal agencies, organizations, schools, and Party branches to fly flags in commemoration on this day and send representatives to participate in the assembly.

Notice of Meeting

To all concerned: September 9th is the anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's First Uprising. Urgently Raised Loan of 143,000 Yuan for Disaster Relief; Banks to Sign First

The Shanghai Fundraising Association for Flood Relief in Various Provinces has negotiated with Shanghai banks for a loan of 500,000 yuan to cover immediate relief efforts. The loan agreement for 300,000 yuan from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications has already been signed, and funds can be withdrawn from the three banks at any time as needed. As for the 200,000 yuan from the member banks of the Bankers' Association, the association has made every effort to persuade the member banks to contribute, and 143,000 yuan has already been pledged. The association is continuing to persuade banks to make up the shortfall. Because this loan is for urgent relief, the association copied the amount pledged by each member bank, along with the agreed-upon loan agreement format, and sent it to the relief association yesterday by letter. The relief association will then finalize the agreements and sign them with the banks that have pledged funds. The loan term is six months, and funds can be withdrawn directly from each bank at any time after the agreements are signed.

Yesterday (the 6th), this newspaper received the following donations for flood relief in various provinces: Xu Huang Haide, 30 yuan (one check from Commercial Savings Bank, No. B3446157); Peng Shaoqu, 20 yuan; Situ Zheng, Li Yinji, Li Anji, 10 yuan each; Lü Yinghao, Zhou Zongye, 5 yuan each; Student Self-Government Association of Jinglin Elementary School, Shi Danxian, anonymous (receipt no. 7353), Wu Zhenying, Lei Yutian, Mai Guo, 2 yuan each; Luo Futang, Guo Jinghu, Lin Changjun, Zhu Baokang, Wang Genmei, Zhu Yufeng, Qiang Guanfu, Lin Changsong, Luo Guangtian, Qu Bogao, 1 yuan each, totaling 132 yuan.

Speech by Li Liejun: Wishes the People of China to Strive for Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Teachings; Plans to Reside in Wuxi and Attend the Plenary Session

According to the Central News Agency, Central Committee member Li Liejun has been recuperating in Qingdao since May, and his health has gradually improved. With the Sixth Plenary Session about to open, he returned to Shanghai on the 5th to prepare to attend in Peking. He then learned that the Sixth Plenary Session had been postponed to November 1st, so he plans to reside in Wuxi for a short time. He has already sent personnel to Wuxi to find suitable housing in the Yuantouzhu area. Li met with reporters from various newspapers at his private residence on Masinan Road on the morning of the 6th and made the following remarks: (Question) Will you attend the Sixth Plenary Session? Do you have any proposals? (Answer) I originally planned to travel to Peking in the coming days to attend the plenary session, but since the session has been postponed, I will return to the mountains to recuperate. I have studied the proposals. What I emphasize is self-reliance. (Question) What is the current situation of Mr. Feng Huanzhang? It is said that he has a proposal for the plenary session that he entrusted to you to bring to Peking. Is that true? (Answer) Mr. Feng is concerned about the country and the people, and is diligent in his studies, as always. I am in regular communication with Mr. Feng. Huanzhang has prepared a proposal, the gist of which is as reported in the newspapers. At the meeting, personnel will be sent from Taishan to Peking to deliver it. I am not currently going to Taishan, so there may be a misunderstanding. Li also said, "The greatest danger facing our country today is the dispersal of people's hearts and the failure to unite national strength. Dr. Sun Yat-sen spoke of this in the past, and he also explained the method of salvation. Therefore, if we seek self-reliance, we must still work hard on Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings and the policies he set forth. If there is a need for me to serve, I will of course do my best."

New Desheng Steamer; Reception and Tour Yesterday; Maiden Voyage to Hong Kong and Guangzhou Tomorrow Morning

After returning to Shanghai from its maiden voyage to Qingdao, the British Jardine Matheson Shipping Company's new Hai Lun Desheng was docked at the Shuntai Wharf. Yesterday, various circles in the city were invited to visit the ship and were treated to tea and refreshments. The ship is scheduled to set sail tomorrow morning (the 8th) on its maiden voyage to Hong Kong, Guangzhou, and other places. The ship's facilities and fares are listed below:

Tonnage and Facilities

The Desheng steamer was built by the Glasgow Govan Company in England, with a length of 310 feet, a width of 48 feet, a draft of 18 feet 6 inches, a displacement of 5,513 tons, a net tonnage of 1,995 tons, a gross tonnage of 3,468 tons, a cargo capacity of 4,376 tons, and a speed of 14.25 nautical miles. The cabins include six A-deck special-class cabins, 26 first-class berths, and 28 second-class berths. The special-class and first-class cabins each have a large dining room, and the decorations are very beautiful. The anti-theft equipment has been carefully considered and is extremely complete.

Schedule and Fares

The ship's schedule for Qingdao, Hong Kong, and Guangzhou is as follows: it departs Shanghai for Qingdao every Saturday and returns to Shanghai from Qingdao the following Tuesday. It then departs Shanghai for Guangzhou every Saturday and returns to Shanghai from Guangzhou the following Friday. The one-way fares are as follows: Shanghai to Qingdao, first class 16 yuan, second class 14 yuan, third class 7 yuan, fourth class 3 yuan; Shanghai to Guangzhou, first class 35 yuan, second class 22 yuan, third class 11 yuan, fourth class 6.5 yuan. It also stops at Shantou and Hong Kong to pick up passengers and cargo.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Haiyi Steamer; Sailed to Haiphong Yesterday; Ye Chuanfang Went to Peking to Obtain International Safety Certificate

The state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Haiyi steamer, acting as an agent for the China Merchants Steamship Company, sailed to Haiphong yesterday morning at 10:00 AM after being inspected and certified by the Hong Kong maritime authorities. The Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Communications sent technician Wang to board the ship at the Jinliyuan Wharf for inspection. The inspection was completed at around 11:00 AM. The cargo, consisting of approximately 3,000 tons of cotton yarn, cotton cloth, flour, and sundry goods, had already been loaded. The ship left port for Haiphong at 4:00 PM in the afternoon, passing through the ports of Xiamen, Shantou, Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Haikou, and Beihai, stopping at all ports except Shantou. It is scheduled to arrive in Haiphong on the 17th and return to Shanghai from Haiphong on the 18th. Ye Chuanfang, manager of the China Merchants Steamship Company, took the Shanghai-Peking night express train to Peking yesterday afternoon at 11:00 AM to obtain the Haiyi Steamer's International Maritime Safety Certificate from the Ministry of Communications. After obtaining the certificate, it will be sent by airmail to the Guangzhou China Merchants Branch and then to the shipowner for safekeeping in order to sail to Haiphong. The passenger fares are contracted by business director Chen Zhuoting, but the cabin crew are directly employed by the company and paid wages, and extortion is strictly prohibited.

Stamp Tax Ambiguity Incident; Suspension of Inspection and Penalties

Chamber of Commerce Telegraphed Ministry of Finance for Adoption

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday, stating: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, the association has repeatedly telegraphed your ministry requesting clarification on various points of ambiguity regarding the stamp tax law. We have also read a special dispatch from Nanjing in the local newspapers of the 3rd, stating that your ministry is currently considering opinions on this matter and will submit them to the Executive Yuan for review and referral to the Legislative Yuan. This shows your utmost sincerity in seeking convenience for the people through careful and thorough consideration. Before a uniform interpretation and approval of these types of incidents is circulated, we request that your ministry order the inspection personnel in all areas to temporarily suspend the inspection of documents under consideration. If they have already been inspected, temporarily suspend the submission for review. If they have already been submitted for review, request that the court temporarily suspend acceptance. Even if the Legislative Yuan's interpretation in the future considers them subject to stamping, they should be allowed to pay the required rate as a supplement and not be penalized for tax evasion. This would be consistent with your ministry's intent to seek fairness and impartiality. We respectfully request that you review, approve, adopt, and implement this proposal. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Kong Xiangxi Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Morning; Talked About His Inspection of the Yellow River Disaster

According to the Central News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, recently went to Shandong to inspect the Yellow River disaster and returned to Peking the day before yesterday. He took the night train to Shanghai that evening and arrived at the North Station at 7:15 AM yesterday morning. He immediately went to his private residence on West Ain Street for rest. At noon, he went to the Central Bank to handle important matters and met with reporters, making the following remarks:

Three Main Reasons for Inspecting the Yellow River Disaster

As the Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council, responsible for water conservancy affairs, I have been concerned about the successive disasters of the Yangtze River and the Yellow River. After inspecting the Yangtze River upstream last time, I returned east and immediately decided to continue to Shandong to inspect the Yellow River disaster. There were three main reasons for this trip north: (1) To communicate the opinions on Yellow River prevention between Jiangsu and Shandong provinces. After arriving in Xuzhou, I invited Shao Hanyuan, Commissioner of Xuzhou, to accompany me to inspect the flood in Shandong Province and introduced Shao to Chairman Han of Shandong to discuss everything. (2) To represent the central government in expressing its concern for the displaced people and to comfort the disaster-stricken elders. (3) To discuss with Chairman Han of Shandong measures to block the breaches and provide emergency relief. This inspection trip north made me feel optimistic about the future of our country. For example, the people provided their own dry food and worked hard on the projects. Even after suffering a great calamity, they did not complain or blame others. As for the civil servants in various places, from the provincial chairman down to the commissioners and county magistrates, they were able to share the joys and sorrows of the people and work hard to rescue them. The troops along the Jinpu Railway have always been disciplined, and the army and the people have a good relationship. This time, they also participated in the flood control projects, which shows that the army and the people have truly become one.

Diversion to Qufu; Reverently Visited the Lin Temple

This year was the birthday of the late teacher Confucius, and I originally planned to go to Shandong to visit the temple, but I was unable to do so due to busy official duties. This time, I took the opportunity to go to Yanzhou and diverted to Qufu to reverently visit the Lin Temple. The garrison in Yanzhou is Sun Tonghuang's troops. Commander Sun's troops have always been known for their discipline, and after stationing in Yanzhou, they implemented a military-industrial policy, filling in the stinking water pit next to the Yanzhou Station and rebuilding it into a garden. They also established the Jindehui to have fun with the people. The road from Yanzhou to Qufu is wide, flat, and smooth, and it was also built by Sun's soldiers. All of this is enough to show the progress of our country. This is what I am pleased and comforted by after inspecting the devastation and suffering caused by the great disaster.
