Consoling Smokers

— Yinghua

Those who do not smoke often look down upon and belittle those who do, seeing them as lacking resolve, ambition, lazy, cowardly, and unwilling to quit. Even if they can quit temporarily, they eventually return to smoking, showing they are content with being inferior and have no desire to improve. Smokers are deeply saddened by such words, filled with grievances but dare not argue, as no one would believe them. Thus, they harbor resentment, and the feelings of smokers and anti-smokers can never be reconciled. This also creates an invisible obstacle to the implementation of tobacco policies. I will first speak on behalf of smokers to redress their grievances, then sincerely advise and persuade them, providing them with a foolproof remedy, so that they will be delighted and sincerely willing to extricate themselves.

The reason why it is difficult for smokers to quit, and the pain of quitting and then relapsing, is nothing more than three points. I dare to explain on their behalf as follows: 1. Of those compatriots who unfortunately fall into the clutches of the "black demon," 99% do so due to illness. The origins of the illness vary, but they largely involve liver and stomach pain, intercostal neuralgia, abdominal pain, muscle and bone pain, hemorrhoids, dysentery, hernia, nocturnal emission, insomnia, neurasthenia, cough, asthma, hemoptysis, bloating, indigestion, deficiency syndrome, constipation, etc.

Opium is originally the most effective remedy for pain, diarrhea, aiding digestion, and promoting blood circulation. It is especially necessary for cholera (vomiting and diarrhea). Pity that some use it often, solely relying on it for treatment, which easily leads to addiction. Therefore, many people in Europe and America are addicted to morphine (morphine is the essence of opium; Westerners do not use lamps and pipes to smoke, but prefer to inject or swallow morphine). If they don't use it for a day, all their illnesses recur, much like the withdrawal symptoms of the Chinese. Yawning, runny nose, tearing eyes, sweating, itchy throat causing cough, cold back, cramping pain in limbs and shoulders, urinary incontinence, even nocturnal emission, an extremely uncomfortable sensation in the kidneys, as if millions of ants are crawling in the blood vessels, bloating in the stomach, inability to eat, involuntary bowel movements, suddenly emptying and lying in feces, impaired sight and hearing, complete loss of memory, and the temporary recurrence of various old illnesses. The most common phenomenon is that smokers, upon waking up, feel lazy and颓唐 because the effects of the opium have worn off. Their limbs are unable to move, their speech is slow and difficult, and their liver becomes hyperactive and prone to anger, with family members and servants often subjected to unwarranted scolding. This is what non-smokers should witness. Considering that smokers are trapped in such a myriad of sufferings, shouldn't we be more understanding and tolerant of their inability to quit easily? 2. Most smokers gradually fall into poverty due to wasted time and loss of employment, experiencing the pain of difficult living conditions. They are also afraid of the government's strict laws and the extortion by unscrupulous ruffians. Who wouldn't want to quit smoking to escape this great burden? However, it is difficult to find doctors who can help quit smoking. Those who advertise in the market are merely speculators trying to make money, without adequate knowledge or skills. Some young and inexperienced practitioners use rapid quitting methods, only treating the symptoms, failing to understand the pain of those quitting, and not adopting a gradual reduction method while simultaneously providing fundamental treatment for underlying conditions. Even if, by chance, one encounters a steady and experienced doctor, they still lack safe and appropriate methods, free from negative consequences, and with consideration for aftercare. Therefore, although they may abstain for a while, they develop symptoms of edema and虚胖. Internally, various illnesses are brewing. Sooner or later, within three to five months, they will develop serious illnesses and strange sores, for which all medicines are ineffective. Only a little opium can immediately relieve the symptoms. This phenomenon is commonly known as "relapse." Famous European and American experts specializing in the treatment of drug addiction also acknowledge this (there are many theories from foreign famous doctors, which will be translated and published successively for public viewing). 3. Doctors charge at least tens of dollars for helping people quit smoking. How can the poor afford such expenses at once? Therefore, they would rather endure the burden of "interest-bearing" smoking, spending two or three 角 a day to prolong their lives. Since the advent of Kang Le Su (康樂素), the above problems have been readily solved. For opium-addicted compatriots, it is like encountering a savior from the brink of death, a treasure raft in the sea of suffering. It has been proven through repeated experiments to be the only wonderful product to assist in quitting smoking. It is peaceful and nourishing, without any adverse side effects. It allows for a gradual quitting method, without suffering any pain. After abstaining for a certain period, it still benefits the Qi and blood, enhances the spirit, and allows the body to gradually become healthier and disease-free. Therefore, there is no relapse, and no future troubles are guaranteed. Moreover, at the beginning of quitting, there is no need to immediately abstain from smoking (referring to licensed smokers). They can assess their physical strength and financial resources to determine the speed of reducing opium consumption (Kang Le Su combined with Fen Jing Shen (奮精神) ensures no pain during smoking reduction). How convenient is that! Strive, gentlemen! You can prosper! The country's survival depends on your joint efforts to save it.

Swimming Training Illustrated Guide Published: Compiled by Yu Binqi, Price 5 Jiao

China's swimming technology has lagged behind due to outmoded methods. Now, the Qinyi Bookstore at 392 Father Luo Shen Road in the French Concession of this port, in order to promote swimming technology, has specially invited swimming expert Mr. Yu Binqi to compile a swimming training book with illustrations, which has already been published. The book collects more than a hundred swimming photos, which is a great effort and is very valuable. The outline is described as follows: Chapter 1: Land Exercises; Chapter 3: Backstroke, Back Ice; Chapter 4: Breaststroke; Chapter 5: Competition and Starting; Chapter 6: Swimming Techniques of Famous Athletes; Chapter 7: Important Points to Note for Competitive Athletes; Chapter 8: Fancy Diving. The difference between this book and general swimming training methods is that general swimming training methods focus on text, with illustrations as supplements. This book focuses on illustrations, with text as a supplement. Practicing according to the illustrations is very clear and easy. The entire book is a paperback, 16-open volume, priced at 5 jiao. The bookstore at 277 Fourth Malu Road in the British Concession of this port also sells it at the same price.

Ministry of Education Orders Sichuan Education Department to Pay Attention to the Improvement of Chongqing University

The Ministry of Education recently, based on inspection reports, issued an order to the Sichuan Education Department. The original order stated, "After checking Chongqing University, the Ministry sent personnel to inspect it. According to recent reports, after further review, the school's operations are of considerable scale and should be approved as a provincial institution. However, the following points must be followed and improved. 1. The school should first establish the Colleges of Science and Engineering. When funding is sufficient, a medical college may be added. There are too few students in the Mathematics and Physics departments of the College of Science. They should be merged into the Department of Mathematics and Physics. The Chemistry Department should remain the same. The College of Engineering should establish three departments: Civil Engineering, Mining and Metallurgy, and Electrical Engineering. Students from the Provincial College of Engineering should be merged into this college, and the funding should also be allocated to this school for overall distribution. The equipment and faculty of the Colleges of Science and Engineering should be strengthened to facilitate teaching. In addition, the school's sports facilities are relatively complete. When necessary, a sports training program may be added. 2. The school's original students have not been reported to the Ministry for registration. They should all be screened by the Education Department and submitted to the Ministry for approval. Students from the Colleges of Liberal Arts and Agriculture should be merged into National Sichuan University. The rest should remain at the school and be properly assigned according to the approved grade level. 3. The school has the position of Vice-President, which is inconsistent with current laws and regulations and should be abolished immediately. In the future, the president of the school should be a full-time position. 4. The admission qualifications of the school's current students are not in compliance with the Ministry's regulations, and the admission process is too lenient. In the future, when recruiting new students, the qualifications should be carefully reviewed, and the standards should be raised, and the admission process should be strict. It is hereby ordered that the department forward this order to ensure that it is strictly followed and reported."

Little Boy (30)(8)

— Original by American Ms. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

Tao Ting was so shocked by the last sentence that he almost fell into the river. He grabbed the window sill, his eyes wide open, looking inside as if he were a taxidermied owl placed on the fireplace mantle in the room. No one dared to disobey when Mr. Pei said so. So Nai De took the stick, looking shocked and guilty as if he was about to stab his teacher to death. He lightly struck the outstretched hand twice. Then he stopped, looking up, his eyes filled with tears, unable to see clearly, but Mr. Pei said without changing his expression, "Again, hit harder."

As if seeing that this was inevitable and eager to get this difficult matter over with quickly, Nai De dragged his sleeve across his eyes and quickly struck two more heavy blows, his hand immediately turning red, but the one wielding the stick felt even more distressed.

"Isn't that enough?" he asked, but he could hardly breathe.

"Mr. Pei only replied, 'Two more'," so Nai De did as he was told, almost not knowing where he was hitting, then he threw the stick hard to the other side of the house, hugged the hand that had been hit with both hands, and sobbed with feelings full of love, respect, shame, and regret:

"I will remember! Oh, I definitely will!"

Mr. Pei then embraced him, changing his firm tone to a sympathetic one, and said:

"I think you will. May God help you, and strive to avoid making us have such an awkward scene again."

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Qiulang)

The ancients said, "Spring and autumn have many good days," and yes: festivals like "Qixi," "Mid-Autumn Festival," and "Double Ninth Festival" in autumn are not all good festivals and auspicious days? But these are only for the bourgeoisie and the leisured class to enjoy in time, as for those poor people, they are too busy making a living, how can they have this leisure and elegance! Especially the survivors of the disaster area, although they escaped death in the rolling torrent, their two major needs of "clothing" and "food" have no whereabouts as autumn and winter are approaching, how can they continue to survive? Perhaps sooner or later they will become starving corpses and frozen ghosts, thinking of this, how can it not make people's hearts ache!

"Autumn wind and autumn rain are heartbreaking," this is the famous sentence left by Qiu Jin, a female knight of Jian Lake. Originally, autumn scholars are mostly sentimental, and their ambitions are not fulfilled, how can they bear the invasion of wind and rain, and be driven into an atmosphere of sorrow and misery, so that he has nowhere to vent, and can only compose them into words and sentences for people to chant. Words are the voice of the heart, and emotions change with the environment. The number of autumn female knights in the world is truly like the sands of the Ganges!

Autumn

— Zhao Gengti

In the past, Dongpo's wife, on a clear spring night with plum blossoms in full bloom, said, "Spring moon is better than autumn moon. Autumn moon makes people feel miserable, and spring moon makes people feel harmonious. You can call Zhao Delin and his fellows to drink under these flowers." It provoked old Dongpo to say such poetic words for his wife, so he proudly wrote: "Light wind and thin mist are all places where young people can enjoy themselves, unlike autumn light, which only illuminates the broken heart of parting people." Here, the bleakness of autumn colors and the faint sorrow scattered in the world were all obliterated in their elegant conversation.

However, there are also some self-admiring people who, when poor and bored, still wear a contemptuous smile and satirize the actions of those who are obsessed with fame and fortune, worried about gains and losses, and hurriedly pursue what is but the achievement of snails on horns, and the ephemeral bubble. Instead, they praise "autumn scenery, every item is a good sentence." Generally, optimistic people do not want to see this thin autumn face. And the so-called commoners, do not have to be virtuous gentlemen, as long as they have habits that are out of step with the world, often have a green method of feeling sad about autumn, and those people only make people worry about their eternal frustration, unable to be lifted up.

Occasionally looking up, there are fleeting white clouds riding on the evening glow, inadvertently passing by, decorating the phoenix trees in this exquisite residential area, which have already revealed one or two haggard yellow spots. I suddenly blurted out: "The evening clouds carry two homeward flights urgently, going to make a night of sorrow by the west window." And a gust of cool wind stirred the thin summer clothes, and with it came a desolate feeling, attacking my brow. But I immediately became alert, as someone who floats and sinks with the world, I am definitely not worthy of imitating the commoners, chanting what "white lotus makes flowers, the wind is already autumn." And that kind of doomed frustrated fate seems to be intolerable in this world. Moreover, as long as one is not deaf and blind, one should also recognize the gradual decline of one's own race. Not washed away by the flood, not committing suicide because of unbearable hunger, in such a high-spirited season, taking advantage of the late dusk, quietly reading a volume or two of books, whether it is Zhuang Zhou's licentiousness or Lao Tzu's purity, that is already too lucky, too lucky! Furthermore, since I cannot bear the heavy responsibility of governing the country and securing the people, nor am I willing to quietly spend some ordinary days, but I come to play the old tune of lamenting autumn with white hair, provoking some unnecessary idle sorrows, I ask, who dares to do that?

Greeting Autumn

— Lan Shan

Once, under the continuous sad wind and miserable rain, in the hawking of hot cabbage blowing in front of the window, erratic and intermittent, touching people's hearts, as if warning me: "Hey! Autumn has come again!"

A slight chill ran down my body, although this is not yet cold weather.

Looking at the two phoenix trees outside the window, they used to be green and lush, but now they are gradually withering and yellowing. Once the golden wind moves, a few remnant leaves bid farewell to the old branches and fall to the ground, dancing with the wind.

Also from the distant, lonely, and old roof ridge, I saw the sad face of autumn, as if with some pallor, but it was silent and deep.

Autumn drove away the joy and warmth of spring from my heart. It also chased away the uninhibited豪情 (grand feelings) of summer, making people lonely and sentimental, sad and sighing.

It comes with a stern means, but it has no compassion for heaven and people. From now on, thousands of plants and trees will gradually lose their vitality. Even my only companion, these two phoenix trees outside the window, are no exception and are being destroyed.

However, under such a solemn situation, my heart is therefore more and more calm. All the unrestrained moods of the previous season are unconsciously suppressed.

In the lonely autumn night, I stood quietly in front of the window of the bedroom, with a cigarette in my hand, smoking non-stop. Leaning on the railing and looking into the distance, as far as my eyes can see, I occasionally saw a few autumn geese flying south in the azure sky, which is so full of poetic and pictorial meaning!

And autumn is most afraid of nostalgia, which can easily cause unwarranted怅触 (melancholy)! Thinking of the close friends of the past, now separated by the ends of the earth, I can't help but sigh to the autumn wind.

Try to gather up a piece of solid sorrow, settle the desolate heart, raise your eyes to see the clear moon, and sing the Shui Diao Ge Tou softly. I am also afraid that I will have the intention of飘飘有遐举 (rising to immortality), and at this moment, the autumn wind has blown away your sorrows.

Beloved and desolate autumn days! You are the old friend of a pessimistic person like me!

Leaves Fall, Lamenting Autumn

Autumn Night

— Shui Rong

Twilight quietly climbed up the deep eaves, and the noble shadows of the amaranth in the yard faded in the leap of thin dusk. A crow croaked outside the window, and then flew away, skimming over the low roof, and in the distance a chimney exhaled light green smoke.

With a lonely heart, I ran down the broken building. Leaving the door ajar, I strolled out, and a sound of autumn greeted me. I shuddered.

Walking, lonely; there was no one around, no voices. The moon, like a Guangbing (a type of cake) gnawed by a mouse, stayed in the sky boredly; the few stars were squinting, and the Milky Way lay sadly in the center. The sounds of autumn insects and the croaking sounds filled the remaining space of the human world.

The road is long, and the darkness stretches to some unknown place. I turned a corner next to a farmhouse with a hand-operated spinning wheel. Forming an acute angle, a clear stream flowed out. It was like white gauze, filtering the moonlight, and I could see the miraculous pebbles inside clearly.

Staring at the silent stream for a while, my heart was also filtered with general desolation. Suddenly, I walked forward again! This time the pace was no longer leisurely, I seemed to have a purpose.

Finding the place I loved, I sat down. It was next to an ancient tomb, an unnamed tomb. This field of grass was as soft as velvet, hibiscus exuded fragrance, the wind sighed on the ancient pine with a very long shadow, and crickets sang a sad dirge.

I picked some hibiscus to make a pillow, and used the lush grass as a mattress. I wanted to spend the night here under the comfort of nature. Just one night was enough!

Autumn Boudoir Poem

— Selected by Zilan Zhuren

The sweet-scented osmanthus weather is pitiful tonight, the fragrance fills the cloud screen and the heat dissipates, I smile in the tent and first wish you well, remember that my birthday is tomorrow morning.

Sleeping together makes me feel that the embroidered quilt is wide, I don't know that the autumn is deep and the afternoon dream is cold, the most is by the mandarin duck pillow by the window in the morning, the red cheeks have no way to avoid the gentleman's gaze.

A piece of the Milky Way hangs over the autumn city, to worship the double stars by the moon, the heart learns incense and has no other wishes, I wish the gentleman a longer life than the concubine.

The orchid lamp shines on the silver screen, the sound of the jade pestle stops without a sound, the red railing is as cool as water, I open the bead curtain to count the autumn stars.

Begonia flowers bloom on the green steps, the courtyard is full of autumn and the fallen leaves are at the beginning, I snatch the red persimmon leaves from the well railing, and grind the fragrant ink myself to ask the gentleman to write a book.

The green locust shadow turns to the small balustrade, the eight-foot dragon beard jade basket is cold, I open a fan from the red window myself, let him look at the bright moon by the pillow.

Autumn Meanderings

— Chen Liang

Yellow willow leaves fill the creek. Miss Wang standing on that naturally formed "Fairy Right" rock, can no longer have a photo taken by Mr. Lu capturing its reflection. The waterfall constantly pounds down from that mountain hollow every day, even becoming somewhat tiresome to watch. Moreover, after several days of autumn wind and rain, the sounds of monkey cries and pine trees possess a certain melancholic power. Miss Wang, sleeping in her tulle mosquito net at the summer villa, quietly began to long for that autumn dance attire and those palatial ballrooms. How tender and graceful!

Therefore, Miss Wang decided to descend the mountain. Suitcases, luggage, local products... all to be personally escorted to Shanghai by Mr. Lu on a later date. Before leaving, Miss Wang gave Mr. Lu an autumn-wave-like glance, expressing her gratitude.

"Shanghai North Station," as the express train pulled into the platform, porters wearing red Turkish hats frantically jumped onto the train. "First-class seat," Miss Wang was helped off the train by a middle-aged man wearing "professor glasses." Upon exiting the station, she was helped into a cream-yellow, streamlined sports car suited for autumn. Driving to the Rising Sun Building, they were stopped by a red traffic light. The man wearing "professor glasses" took the cigar from his lips, smiled and said, "What do you think of Shanghai's atmosphere? Doesn't feel unfamiliar, does it?" Miss Wang cast a sidelong glance: "Shanghai is, after all, Shanghai!" She looked at the "Autumn Grand Sale" posters plastered on the glass windows of large companies, twitching her right leg resting on her left.

Turning west from Nanjing Road, the plane tree leaves on both sides of Jing'an Temple Road also appeared withered. A few were blown onto the gray-white road surface, tumbling before being crushed by the car wheels. The windows of the Grand Hotel slowly changed color, and a whiff of Cuban coffee wafted in through the car window. Miss Wang wrinkled her nose: "I wonder which place has good music these days. I'll go there tonight, that 'New Foxtrot' has become a little rusty."

Under the green lights, amidst the intoxicating fragrance, on the springy dance floor, floated an autumnal dance dress of silver satin inlaid with bright white mirror and black trim. An old dance enthusiast said: "Miss Wang is making her first appearance since the weather turned cooler." The dance hall manager said: "From now on, this place will be lively again!"

Old Feelings in New Autumn

— Yafei

The wheel of time ceaselessly turns. That lovely yet hateful summer has quietly slipped away, and this pensive autumn has also silently descended. Thus, years of old wounds and new scars stir again in my broken heart. At the same time, the lake of my heart, which had been as still as stagnant water for so long, cannot help but ripple once more.

The first thing that will make me forever feel lonely on the path of life is the shattering of my peace. Its destruction took away my lively heart, shattered my beautiful dreams, and plunged my life into a heavy shade of gray.

I remember last year, also in autumn, I happily embarked on my journey home, dreaming of returning to my hometown. At that time, my sister An knew that her only younger brother was coming home, so she specially put aside all household chores and rushed to the riverbank to wait for me. When she saw me, how happy she was, how excited! I believe this kind of joy and excitement had never been revealed in her heart since adulthood. Especially that slight smile, the meaning contained in that smile could never be analyzed by superficial people. She knew I loved to eat fresh water chestnuts, so she sent a load of fresh water chestnuts just picked from the lake.

When I got home, I couldn't say anything. So, for a long period of time, we remained silent. There was not a single word that could express our inner thoughts. After years of separation, once we met, we felt relatively silent. That pure, warm feeling did not get a chance to be unleashed, and was only conveyed in our mutual silence. They hoped for me, expected me to bring back some glory and success. But what did I bring back? A few inexpensive items of luggage, an already weakened body, an elderly person's state of mind, and a young man's pale face! I was truly ashamed to see them. However, at the same time, I felt unspeakable gratitude. Gratitude made me unable to stop the hot tears from hanging down from my withered cheeks. I wanted to tell them about my situation in the past few years, how much injustice I had suffered, and how much cold treatment I had encountered. But, but how could I say it, how could I bear to say it! They hoped for me, they expected me, and I finally returned with boundless disappointment! I really wanted to cry. I wanted to throw myself into my kind mother's arms like a child suffering from injustice, and cry bitterly, to exchange for her kind comfort, to caress my wounded soul. But how could I bear to further wound her fragile heart! I still restrained my tears, suppressed my sorrow, and forced myself to put on a cheerful face against my will!

Now it is autumn again. Although I want to go back, how can I bear to go back again? Perhaps by now, the weeds on An's grave have grown several feet long. She sleeps forever underground. How could she know that her wandering younger brother, on a desolate autumn night, is mourning for her in a foreign land... I will respectfully offer a wisp of sorrow at her grave!

Modern Medicine Journal

Measles

— Physician Yu Bofu

Children's birth has two major misfortunes. One is smallpox. The other is measles. However, since the invention of vaccination, smallpox can be avoided. But there is still no way to prevent measles.

Measles is also called rubella, and is also known as the measles rash. Its degree of danger is inversely proportional to age. That is, the younger the age, the greater the danger.

Measles is extremely contagious. The patient's tears, nasal mucus, phlegm, and excrement, clothes and utensils are, of course, contagious. Even the surrounding air and dust, and even the skin shed by the patient when they are about to recover, can be spread by the wind and infect others. Therefore, if measles is discovered nearby, strict isolation is essential.

Patients should avoid meat and fish. Even smelling them can prevent the measles from being properly expressed. Therefore, the wet nurse should also eat vegetarian food. Food should be easily digestible, such as porridge, soup, milk, and eggs. Avoid getting cold, and avoid drafts. If there are accompanying symptoms such as cough, diarrhea, or other symptoms, then hundreds of complications can occur, becoming even more dangerous. It is essential to seek medical treatment.

For those Suffering from Nocturnal Emission

Discussion on the Equal Importance of Abstinence and Semen Retention

— Physician Zheng Huimin

Nocturnal emission is more common among scholars than among warriors, and more common in urban areas than in rural areas. Therefore, it is also known as the scholar's disease and the urban disease. Patients may leak during the night while dreaming, or emit without dreaming. Precious essence, the source of life, flows out incessantly, damaging life and causing disease. Therefore, patients are all terrified and apprehensive, forcibly abstaining in order to prevent leakage. Yet, the emission persists. What is the reason?

According to the theory, nocturnal emission is caused by the relaxation of the vas deferens. The gate of semen is not secure, and the essence is eager to come out. Although abstaining from sex is the usual advice, it is only a superficial treatment. It is necessary to strengthen the gate of semen to get to the root of the problem.

For retaining semen, the most effective formula is "Dr. Schmidt's Semen Retention Tablets," made according to the secret formula of Dr. Schmidt, a German venereal disease expert. The medicine is kingly. It strengthens the gate of semen. I often prescribe it to patients suffering from nocturnal emission. Its effect is invariably seen the same night. It is also a shortcut to treating nocturnal emission.

Treatment of Leukorrhea and Infertility

— Physician Ren Guoxiang

Leukorrhea in women has various causes. Patients have a purulent secretion in the vagina that is highly acidic. When male sperm enters, it is immediately destroyed. If pregnancy is desired for the sake of succession, there is absolutely no hope.

However, women are bound by old ethical teachings. If they suffer from leukorrhea, they often keep it a secret and dare not seek medical treatment, considering it shameful. On the one hand, it endangers their own health and happiness. On the other hand, pregnancy is hopeless, which is truly pitiable.

Therefore, self-treatment is convenient for women suffering from leukorrhea. The advent of "Leukorrhea Remedy" for self-treatment of leukorrhea is truly a great blessing for female patients.

Various Aspects of Menstruation

— Physician Zhao Zhigao

Menstruation refers to the uterine bleeding that occurs in women approximately every twenty-eight days from the time puberty begins until the time it permanently ceases.

Its color is dark red, like venous blood. The average amount is about three taels (approximately 100 ml). Its properties, besides containing secretions from the uterus and vagina, mucus from the cervix, and a large number of bacteria, are no different from the blood in the human body.

The origin of menstruation is the congestion of the mucosal epithelium on the inner surface of the uterus due to the pressure of ovarian rupture stimulation. As congestion continues, it gradually peels off. Small blood vessels also rupture, resulting in bleeding. This is what is called menstruation.

Hygiene is most important during menstruation. Avoid sexual intercourse, labor, travel, dancing, and overeating. It is best to rest quietly. Locally, a menstrual belt made of cotton or gauze can be used to absorb the discharged menstrual blood. Do not make it too tight. If it is too tight, it will cause a blockage, and menstrual blood will not be able to flow out, accumulating in the vagina and causing putrefactive vaginitis. In the old customs of our country, women often used coarse cloth and rough paper during menstruation. It was filthy and inferior, the absorbent power was weak, and there were many bacteria. Paper scraps entered the vagina, often causing vaginitis and other symptoms, which is extremely unsanitary.

Treatment of Neurasthenia

— Zhou Xiaohan, Physician

(Symptoms) Headache, heaviness of the head, pessimism in everything, forgetfulness, mood swings, insomnia, nervousness, back pain, lower back pain, excessive sweating, cold hands and feet, palpitations, cold sensations or hot flashes, weakness throughout the body, rapid pulse, fatigue, frequent urination, premature ejaculation, spermatorrhea, nocturnal emission, and weakness (the latter four are specifically called sexual neurasthenia).

(Causes) Malnutrition, excessive use of the brain and little physical activity, excessive mental stimulation, sexual overexertion, excessive masturbation, endocrine disorders, chronic poisoning, and weakness after illness.

Shenbao Radio Weekly

Review of Coil Issues

— Ming

——Using Iron Core Coils——

The necessary conditions for a perfect radio include high sensitivity, good selectivity, balanced amplification of signals of different high and low pitches, and a large signal-to-noise ratio. Of course, any part of the radio can affect these many conditions, but the design of the coil is particularly important.

Most of the current radios are five-tube, and their coordination is exemplified as follows: One – oscillation and first wave detection mixing stage, commonly using 6A7 vacuum tube; one – intermediate amplification stage, using 78 or 6D6 tube; one – second wave detection and automatic address control mixing stage, using 75 tube; and one – audio frequency output stage, using 41 or 42 tube. (The same is true when using 2.5V vacuum tubes.) This type of radio, due to the limitation of the number of vacuum tubes, only has one intermediate amplification stage, so the total amplification force needs to be increased as much as possible, which can also improve selectivity. After this point can be satisfactorily resolved, the remaining problems are the design of the antenna stage and the oscillation stage coils, and how to improve the performance of the radio.

When designing the oscillation killing coil, because it is necessary to consider location and economy, small superimposed ones are often used. If a single-layer coil with a large diameter can be used instead, the performance will of course be better, but the improvement can only enhance the sensitivity, and the solution of the remaining conditions must rely on the antenna coil.

The antenna coils currently wound in radios are extremely small, especially those with isolation shields, which significantly weaken the efficiency. The only remedy is to use a diagonal superimposed winding method in the hope of slightly reducing losses.

The loss of the coil is enough to limit the improvement of its sensitivity and selectivity. Therefore, to design an ideal coil, it is necessary to first analyze the causes of coil loss and then seek ways to eliminate them. The main causes of coil loss can be divided into the following three items:

1. Through-sensing body loss between insulation layers

2. Eddy current loss of conductors and isolators

3. Resistance loss of the conductor itself

(1) The source of through-sensing body loss is due to the inevitable existence of capacitance between conductors. Therefore, this capacitance must be reduced to a minimum. If an appropriate diagonal cross-winding coil can be used, this loss can be expected to be reduced to a minimum. The more times each turn is crossed, the smaller the loss. One crossing is sufficient for long-wave radio coils, but because broadcast radio has a higher frequency, the through-sensing body loss is greater, and four or five crossings per turn are required to be satisfactory. Another method to reduce through-sensing body loss is to use double-layer silk-covered wire to increase the thickness of the green insulation layer and reduce its capacitance, which can naturally reduce the loss.

(2) The method to reduce the eddy current loss of the conductor is to use stranded wire twisted from many fine wires, each of which is insulated with enamel. For the eddy current loss of insulators, materials with lower resistance, such as copper, aluminum, and zinc, can also be selected, and the distance between them and the coil can be increased to reduce it.

(3) In order to solve the problem of resistance loss of the conductor itself, I don't know how much brainpower wireless engineers have spent. It is generally believed that to reduce resistance loss, the coil with the specified inductance should be shortened as much as possible, and attention should be paid to the medium in the coil. It is necessary to select a substance with greater magnetic induction than air to compensate for the weakening of the coil's inductance and still maintain the specified value.

For many years, many engineers have wanted to implement the structure of a power transformer on a high-frequency coil. They have tested various iron sheets, iron filings, and fine iron wires as the iron core of the coil. Although each test has achieved considerable improvement, the extremely high broadcast frequency current, eddy current losses would inevitably occur, resulting in more harm than good.

Comparatively speaking, iron filings are the most satisfactory, but they must be broken down into extremely small particles, almost visible under a microscope, and each particle must be separately insulated. This complex and difficult device can only be tested in large-scale laboratories and cannot be used for widespread commercial use. In short, the manufacture of iron-core coils is still in its infancy and awaits future improvements.

Key Points for Making AC Radios

— Zhou Wende

DC radios are inconvenient to use, and the monthly battery cost is around two yuan. Therefore, amateur enthusiasts generally prefer to make AC radios. If an AC radio is easy to make and has excellent sound quality, that goes without saying. However, if the construction method is slightly incorrect, many problems will arise. Now, I will write down a few key points gained from experience for fellow enthusiasts:

(1) When making an AC radio, the arrangement of all components has a great impact. Loud AC hum is very annoying. Based on experience, when installing, do not fix them with screws or solder. Connect them only with copper wires and test the sound. If the sound is poor, you can rearrange them and test the sound until you get the best method, and then fix them. Otherwise, if you fix them with screws and solder first, it will be very inconvenient to remove the screws and solder after testing if you find it unsatisfactory.

(2) When making, be careful to prevent metal objects from falling in, otherwise short circuits can easily occur. At least there will be no sound, and at worst the entire machine will be damaged. Be sure to be careful.

(3) When we make transformerless AC radios (such as using 25Z5 vacuum tubes as transformer substitutes), we must be especially careful because it is easy to get an electric shock. It is best to keep it in an insulated wooden box to avoid danger.

(4) The components used in the construction must be checked one by one for broken wires, short circuits, or other damaged parts. Sometimes one broken thing is enough to affect the entire machine.

(5) When making an AC radio, danger may occur due to the destruction of the wires or short circuits in the transformer. Therefore, it is best to add a switch and a fuse to the wires during testing to prevent danger.

(6) When making, you must first know whether the power supply to the radio matches the transformer you want to install. For example, the power supply in the French Concession is 110V, and the power supply in the International Settlement is 220V. If you use a 220V primary transformer with a 110V power supply, or use a 110V primary transformer with a 220V power supply, danger will occur.

(7) The wiring of AC radios must have surface insulation, as even a slight short circuit is very dangerous.

(8) The fixed capacitors (FixedCondinser) used in AC radios are mostly those that can withstand high-voltage current. Do not confuse them with the paper fixed capacitors used in DC radios, which can cause danger. Therefore, it is best to consult a radio supply store or someone with experience before making.

(9) The vacuum tubes used in AC radios are specific. For example, 30, 31, and other vacuum tubes are used in DC machines and are not suitable for AC radios. The ones used in AC radios must be AC vacuum tubes or AC/DC vacuum tubes. Therefore, do not make a mistake.

Amateur Musings (Continued)

— Wu Yingjian

Last winter, I made an AC four-tube radio, and I thought the results were quite good. I used it for a long time and never had any problems, nor were any parts damaged. But once, the variable resistor for adjusting the volume suddenly lost its effect. When rotating the volume knob, the volume could not be gradually increased or decreased. It was either loud or silent. Later, I took it apart and saw that most of the carbon material inside had fallen off. I tried to apply it carefully with a pencil, but it didn't work. I always felt uncomfortable in my heart, and I had to find a replacement method to feel at ease. Where there's a will, there's a way. As a result, I found a very good volume adjustment method. The original machine had a tone adjuster connected to the screen grid of the power amplifier tube, as shown in the figure. Originally, it was a series connection of a .02MF fixed capacitor and a 50,000-ohm variable resistor. Now, I replaced the .02MF fixed capacitor with a 1MF fixed capacitor, and it became a very good volume adjuster.

Low Resistivity Fixed Carbon Resistors

— Pao

In the damping circuit, the damping is usually as small as possible. However, sometimes in order to obtain a flatter selectivity curve, a resistor with a small resistivity and no self-inductance is intentionally connected. These resistors have always been specially wound wire-wound resistors with no self-inductance. Because in fact, there are no fixed carbon resistors with low resistivity on the market for use.

Recently, the American Ohiohm factory has produced a set of fixed carbon resistors with a wide variety of types. The resistivity is as low as 0.04 ohms and as high as 100 megohms (100Megohm); the power ranges from one-quarter watt to ten watts; the variety of colors is sufficient for general applications; and fixed carbon resistors with small resistivity, which have always been difficult to buy, can now be purchased.

The appearance of this resistor is the same as that of ordinary fixed carbon resistors. During manufacturing, it was tested under the standards stipulated by the Radio Manufacturers Association (R.M.A.) in the United States, and the results exceeded the qualified standards by a large margin. It is said that it can be used normally even in the harsh climate of the two seasons in the tropics.

Publishing Industry

The Responsibility of Intellectuals to the Publishing Industry

— Zeng Jianping

In recent years, due to the poverty of the general public and the failure of several revolutionary movements in the past, the publishing industry, which once had vitality, has quickly declined. Large bookstores, like the bourgeoisie, have completely become prisoners of feudal landlords and no longer dare to advocate a little bit of progressive revolutionary consciousness: small bookstores, however, have completely exposed the faces of their small property owners and returned to the shadow of taste. This kind of specialized and concrete performance is that some parties are printing their ancient books in large quantities, while others are publishing tempting reading materials that are full of carnal desires. The current trend in the publishing industry completely exposes the suicidal tendencies of Chinese publishing intellectuals—even the national people's lives.

The occurrence and development of this tendency does not seem to be a matter of the last year or two. However, our progressive intellectuals—the writing community and the reading community—are completely silent, not daring to give this tendency a forceful blow: even many writers who have been relatively progressive in the past dare not put forward serious criticisms. Certain publishing organizations are carrying out their restoration, anti-era, and anti-revolutionary movements in a planned way; but progressive readers are adopting a liberal attitude towards this reactionary tendency and movement. They willingly learn to be ostriches, hiding their heads in a place where they cannot see danger. If it is said that today's publishing industry is "equivalent to sending opium to the people" (as Mr. Li Maimai said): then, our intellectuals are no different from tacitly approving the public sale of red pills by those who kill the nation. In recent years, the corruption of the general public's thoughts and the degradation of the general public's lives, our progressive intellectuals should bear a heavy responsibility.

Although the emergence and development of the fashion of an era inevitably has its objective conditions. However, the power to change customs actually relies on the subjective resistance of our progressives. The political depression and economic bankruptcy in China in recent years are enough to create the reactionary, restorationist, and romantic decadent tendencies of the modern publishing and reading communities: but this tendency can be reduced and purged through a broad and powerful resistance movement. If no one wants to read ancient books, the large bookstores that publish ancient books will close or change direction; if no one wants to read pornographic books and comics, the small bookstores that publish pornographic books and comics will inevitably go bankrupt and cannot be supported. The creation of a good atmosphere in the reading community is mainly due to the call of progressive intellectuals: not in the transformation of large and small publishing organizations that aim for profit. If our intellectuals are willing to always learn the ostrich's method; then, where can we talk about the revolutionary cultural movement and the revolutionary national movement!

Therefore, if the current intellectuals in China are not willing to implement chronic suicide in the cultural field, then at this time, we should rise up: from criticism, create a broad critical movement to attack the current reactionary restoration movement; from enlightenment, create a powerful cleansing movement to purge all decadent tendencies that endanger the nation. Actively learn from the Japanese and British people, especially the Russians, and publish systematically small series of books and small libraries in the style of libraries on a large scale. Not only should it be developed from literature, but it should also be developed from the theoretical parts of various departments of natural science and social science. If not, if revolutionary intellectuals only seek temporary safety and leisure, then the development of the publishing industry that is currently publishing ancient books in large quantities will inevitably completely clear the past achievements of our national revolution and cultural revolution, and drag the times back again.

If this era—an era that has gone through several cultural and political revolutions—is dragged back by the current corrupt booksellers and armed men's guests who promote the reading of scriptures with whips: then, the revolutionary intellectuals, at that time, in addition to being guests again, will reduce—no, will disappear—his historical mission and the significance of promoting the era in culture. Therefore, the only way for intellectuals to liberate and save themselves at present is not to surrender to the booksellers who promote the restoration movement and the armed men who promote the reading of scriptures, and resolutely urge the current publishing industry to save our descendants, save the revolution, and save themselves!

Talking About Tools and Reference Books

— Chen Haochu

Whether standing in the position of a reader or the position of a library, we have very sufficient reasons to hope that the publishing industry will pay more attention to the compilation and printing of tools and reference books. The current teaching method is not just to let students read some textbooks to death, but to hope to cultivate students' ability to automatically refer to research: on the other hand, the poor and studious people who are forced to run around for food and clothing all day long, they cannot have a whole day of leisure to go to the library to browse various books, and they also very much hope that there are reference books that can save their energy, so the compilation and publication of tool books is what today's readers unanimously expect.

The scope of reference books is very broad. In a broad sense, all kinds of books have the value and mission of being referenced; here we add the word "tool", which stipulates his narrow scope, that is, only books that are used as tools. This type of reference book, in terms of compilation style, is based on the collection of various facts, arranged and compiled according to law, for the purpose of checking, from the library's point of view, it is usually placed separately, only for readers to check and not to borrow. From the user's point of view, it is not necessary to read carefully at ordinary times, but only to check at the necessary time to assist in the study and advancement of reading and research. According to this strict meaning, the so-called tool reference books are only dictionaries, dictionaries, encyclopedias, type books, chronological tables, yearbooks, indexes, etc. These types of books are what we hope the publishing industry will pay more attention to publishing.

The compilation of tool reference books has a long history in China. "Erya" has the method of dividing sections, and "Shuowen" has the system of radicals, which has evolved to the "Kangxi Dictionary", and dictionaries have almost the same long history as Chinese characters. As for chronological tables, Taishi Gong wrote the "Historical Records" in the early Han Dynasty, and he created the method of parallel oblique lines of the Zhou Genealogy: Wan Sitong's "Chronological Tables of Past Dynasties" and Qi Zhaonan's "Chronological Tables of Past Dynasties" are even more masterpieces of history. During the Wei Wen Emperor period, Wang Xiang and others compiled scriptures and gathered them according to type, and compiled the book "Huanglan", which opened the source of Chinese type books; after that, the compilation became popular in various dynasties, and many were completed. During the Ming Dynasty, Ling Dizhi compiled the "Wanxing Tongpu" in 140 volumes, which dates back to ancient times and the Ming Dynasty. It comprehensively covers the surname and clan system, with rhyme as the priority and dynasty as the order. It also lists the deeds of famous people of past dynasties and assigns them to various surnames according to the era. It is actually a very good dictionary of Chinese personal names; later, the article "Shangyoulu" by people in the Ming and Qing Dynasties imitated the style of this book. Indexes are still a new type of tool book in China, but the "Shixing Yunbian" in 64 volumes edited by Wang Huizu of the Qing Dynasty is an excellent index of personal names in the Twenty-Four Histories. Even today, it is still an indispensable and important tool for checking official history reporters. However, although the compilation of tool reference books has been quite developed in China in the past, few people can make good use of them. In the past, scholars mostly despised tool books, thinking that everyone could do it and it was not worth calling it writing. For example, Wang Huizu's books on historical tools include "Shixing Yunbian", "Jiushi Tong Xingming Lu", and "Liao Jin Yuan Sanshi Tongming Lu". Not only are the volumes numerous, but also the works are extremely meticulous, but in the Qing Dynasty, few people paid attention to them. Ruan Yuan wrote a biography for the teacher, but called it "Biography of Xunli Wang Jun": Zhang Zhidong wrote a book list and asked questions, and adopted five or six kinds of the teacher's books, but at the end of the volume, the names of Qing Dynasty writers were omitted, which can be seen from this. Since tool books are not valued by general scholars, and those who use them are just some shallow-minded candidates, the compilation and utilization of tool books ultimately cannot create a brilliant atmosphere in the Chinese academic circle. (To be continued)

Gleanings from Northern Drama

— Zhao Jingshen

Published by Commercial Press Preface by Lu Qian Ren Ne

It is said that this is a manuscript copy of the Ming Dynasty collected in Tianyi Pavilion, with a total of twenty-seven suites and fifty-four small orders. Ren Ne's preface said: "Jing Shizhen, Chuweizhe, Xichen, Master of Huxi, is not seen in other books... Mis-entered two suites, "Wuru Tiantai" and "Hutoupai", which are different from those recorded in "Yuanqu Xuan" and can be used for comparison. "Qiaoxiaosheng Duan Jiuse Caiqi" is extremely similar to miscellaneous dramas and has four suites, and the official tunes are different, so it is suspected to be the four suites in one drama. It has not been seen in the past in the list of dramas and still needs to be verified... Seven of the twenty-seven suites are found in Yongxi, which has been slightly collated."

This preface is of a textual research nature, and I will pick out three points from what he said to talk about: 1. Is the collation of Hutoupai precise; 2. Is Jiuse Caiqi the name of a miscellaneous drama: 3. Are there only seven suites seen in Yongxi Yuefu?

Regarding the first point, we should forgive Mr. Ren, because he was only "slightly" collated. However, he pays great attention to the separation and combination of tunes, and it seems that negligence in this aspect should not have occurred. For example, he pointed out that "Beiqu Shiyi" should not combine "Shan Shiliu" and "Zuiniangzi" into one tune, which can be used as proof of his attention to the separation and combination of tunes. However, "Man Jinzhan" originally had six short sentences, and "Beiqu Shiyi" mistakenly titled the last four short sentences as "Hutubai", but Mr. Ren did not point it out. Also, the first song of "Bubaimen" is also titled "Xianggong Ai". "Zuiniangzi" is written as "Zui Ye Mosa" in Yongxi. According to the "Beici Guangzhengpu", the two tunes are actually different. There are several different versions of the collation of the second fold of "Hutoupai", such as "Yuanqu Xuan", "Yongxi Yuefu", "Beici Guangzhengpu", and "Beiqu Shiyi". The most interesting thing is the linked suites. "Beiqu Shiyi" lacks the last "Litingyan Sha" and has the previous "Zaoxiang'er", while the other books lack "Zaoxiang'er" and have "Litingyan Sha". In principle, both should be present. The order of the linked suites attached to the end of the "Beici Guangzhengpu" table of contents is listed below, and the other three books are compared: (Yuan stands for "Yuanqu Xuan", Yong stands for "Yongxi Yuefu", and Bei stands for "Beiqu Shiyi")

Wugongyang Luomeifeng Cheng Xiangci (Bei is Zaoxiang'er, Yuan and Yong have none) Anahuman Jinzhan (Bei is divided into Man Jinsheng and Hutubai) Shizhu Zi Dabaimen Shanshi Qiao (Bei is the same, Yuan and Yong are divided into Shan Shiliu and Zuiniangzi) Xiaobaimen (Bei is the same, Yuan and Yong are divided into Xianggong Ai and Bubaimen) Yebuluo Xiaoxirenxin (Yuan, Yong and Bei are all Xirenxin) Zuiniangzi (Bei is the same, Yuan and Yong are Zui Ye Mosa) Yue'erwan Fengrensong (Yuan, Yong and Bei are all Fengliuguan, the second example of the Fengliu style in Beici Guangzheng is Hutoupai, and it is also called Fengrusong in the table of contents, which is contradictory in itself!) Hutubai Tangwudailitingyan with Xiezhi Sha (Bei has none, Yuan is all Litingyan Shi Sha)

Without paying much attention to this collation in the past, after reading it, I felt that the exotic atmosphere was very strong, and the fresh breath was rushing into my face. For example, the libation is not to the sky, but to "pour the libation facing the sun", how cute is this sentence! Others such as bamboo arrows, thread robes, Cigu flute, leather drums, and even "the silver basin is like Pang'er wearing greasy powder makeup, and the inkstone also has a beard wrapped in velvet rope," all have a special flavor. This is a digression, not to be mentioned.

Regarding the second point, my answer is no. Just look at the tone of these four suites and you can tell that they are completely sung by one person. In Yuanqu, it seems that there is no example of a solo play like Jinghe's "Picking Up Gold". As for using Jiuse Caiqi as a drama, we can see the "Four Great Fools" quoted in Jiao Xun's "Drama Talk" Volume 5: "The Four Great Fools Legend of Landscape Neighbors, the wine fool is Jiang Yingzhao who obtains ill-gotten wealth and then ruins his family with wine; the color fool is Zhuangzi fanning the grave, his wife splitting the coffin; the money fool is about Lou Yuanwai's one penny, and the anger fool is Huang Zai rebelling because he failed the exam. The wine fool is also called Jiu Dong, and was written by Li Fengshi of Wulin. Yi Wen Qian is also engraved in the name of a family miscellaneous drama, called a broken miser. Of course, this has nothing to do with "Qiaoxiaosheng Duan Jiuse Caiqi". The money fool is Yi Wen Qian, which itself has more than six acts, see "Sheng Ming Zaju Chu Ji". The Four Great Fools are probably at least more than twenty acts, which cannot be accommodated in four folds. The editor of "Beiqu Shiyi" seems to like the separate chanting of Jiuse Caiqi, like the author of "Jing Hua Yuan" Li Ruzhen. In the same book, he also copied down four "Chu Duizi" that separately chant Jiuse Caiqi (page 43) and also copied down a "Hui'er Luo" with a first song that chants Jiuse Caiqi in unison, carrying over "De Shenglin" (page 47).

Regarding the third black, I also feel that Mr. Ren is slightly negligent. In addition to the seven suites that he cited (Zhengguan Duanzheng Hao Dadawei, Shangdiao Jixian Shi Shu Huai, Cunli Yagu, Nanlu Yizhilian Hua Zeng Yingguo, Xianlu Dian Jiangchun Jing Shizhen Zuo), and Fulu Yizhilian Hua Jianzu, we can also cite two suites, namely: 1. Page 21, "Jin Dian Xi Chongchong" is seen in Yongxi Yuefu Volume 2, page 37: 2. Page 28, Nanlu Yizhilian Hua, is seen in Yongxi Yuefu Volume 10, page 13. I think there are reasons why Mr. Ren did not see these two suites, namely: 1. In Yongxi Volume 2, he only paid attention to the general title of Zhenggong Duanzheng Hao and did not notice that there was still a part that was not Duanzheng Hao, such as "Jin Dian Xi Chongchong", "Fan Ma Wu Xifeng", "Tuobu Shan", "Yijianmei", "Yuezhao Ting", etc.: 2. Yongxi Volume 8, to Volume 10, these three books are all based on Nanlu Yizhilian Hua, he only checked the sentences with exactly the same first sentence, and thought it was okay if there was no "one year old like one year", but he did not know that "this year old like last year" is a variant of "one year old like one year", so he glanced over it.

Also, Ren Ne's preface claims that "Zaoqi'er" uses Xun Xinqi, but the first song of this tune, "Keng Nuan Chuang Ming Caoshe Di" has already been recorded in Beici Guangzhengpu, and is not very rare.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Words

Our Oriental New York

— Jia Wei

This may be something we are very proud and happy about. Our largest city in the country, known as "Oriental New York"—Shanghai—is just thriving! Although the ten-story to twenty-story high-rise buildings are still far from the true New York "skyscrapers" and "soaring pavilions." However, in recent years, the construction of this kind of building, like "bamboo shoots after the rain," is undeniable.

According to a report in the newspaper the other day from Hu Guangshe, "According to news from the Civil Engineering Department of the Public Concession and the French Concession Engineering Bureau, the statistics of construction in the two concessions recently show that the sharp increase in investment in huge buildings is quite alarming. From the second half of last year to the present, there are a total of more than 5,130 large buildings built in the Public Concession. The French Concession is a residential area, and the construction of this new type of building has increased even more sharply. Therefore, according to observations in the construction industry, the completion of Oriental New York is not far away."

However, things cannot be so optimistic. According to a friend who works in a certain national goods company, their company is preparing to open a branch company in a certain department store in the west of the city. The western-style tiled building is quite magnificent. From the first floor to the second floor, it occupies more than a dozen rooms, but it does not need to pay any rent (usually it costs about 600 yuan per month). It is said that the landlord is afraid that "equipment will easily break if it is not used"—"a door hinge does not decay, and flowing water does not stagnate"—so he is willing to make such a generous sacrifice. At the same time, there is a contract for a period of six months. After the expiration of the period, if the company has a profit, it will start to pay the rent.

At first, hearing this kind of thing would make people feel a little strange, but the fact is exactly like this—the atmosphere of "economic downturn" permeates every corner, and no one can deny this. Taking the economic figures of the Public and French Concessions' investment in the construction industry as an example: in 1934, the Public Concession was 35,000,000 yuan, and the French Concession was 16,000,000 yuan. Compared to the 65,287,000 yuan in 1930 (Public) and 18,589,000 yuan (French), the difference is obvious. Moreover, according to the statistics of the Finance Department of the Public Concession Engineering Bureau, the number of vacant houses in a corner of the Public Concession alone increased to more than 6,383 in the summer of last year. (The number in the same period in 1930 was 4,687) If the vacant houses in the French Concession and the Nanshi area are all counted, it is probably no less than 100,000—the investment in the construction industry and the increase and decrease of vacant houses are in inverse proportion—but what about this year?

Now let us excerpt a paragraph from a Shanghai communication published in a certain newspaper in another port: "The Nanjing Road area is the center of the city. Recently, eight or nine out of ten stores have raised the banner of low prices and put up slogans for big sales. Statistics show that there are 18 department stores, 16 silk and satin stores, 7 watch stores, and many other South goods stores, electrical materials, cotton textiles, and leather goods stores. Only a certain incense and candle store next to Taibaosi Temple (ie Hongmiao) does not need to hold low prices due to the increasing number of people who promote superstition in recent years, and it is even overwhelmed with customers. Three or four years ago, it was not easy to rent a house on Nanjing Road for business, and it was necessary to pay a considerable amount of exercise fees. Today, houses for rent are everywhere... The prosperity of the city is gradually declining, which is truly a change of fortune."

Therefore, the sharp increase in huge buildings and structures is only a manifestation of the city's deformed development—the failure of the real estate industry has led entrepreneurs to develop their financial resources towards the "occupying the sky but not the land" high-rise buildings.

The prosperity of our "Oriental New York"—what can I say?

Mid-Autumn Moon

— Ling Zixi

(“The crescent moon shines over the nine provinces, some families are happy, some are sorrowful?”)

As usual, once autumn arrives, the azure sky begins to float with reddish-gold, ever-changing clouds; the sky becomes high and clear, the sea becomes vast; withered, powerless leaves, resentfully sobbing, fall to the ground, in the melancholy of twilight, recalling those good old days; in the distance, some intangible sounds vaguely and indistinctly float… Autumn has irrevocably seeped in.

It's already the time when the moon is round; those who have left the metropolis cannot easily imagine the festive scenes on the streets; perhaps there are still many electric lights and people? (However, I heard that "Mid-Autumn" is also a slightly frightening term for people in the metropolis, it's also a checkpoint), perhaps there is also a beautiful moon…?

Yes, it is a "festival," the moon is round, large, and clear, it casts bronze-colored light through sparse branches onto the front of village houses, onto the small village of "Lujiazhai," like an oil-less lamp, gloomy.

What kind of sigh of life rises up! Those families—fifty or so in the small village, after a flood that was finally somewhat milder, in the moonlight as clear and cold as mountain spring water, vaguely recall the outlines of those good years: autumn, the season of results and harvests, the fragrant rice ears that have ripened, the reward for a year's labor before their eyes, the lovely moon on Mid-Autumn Festival night, folk legends, folk customs and festive scenes, mooncakes, incense holders, piles of food, children's laughter, adults' laughter…

A whole pile! The scene of good years, but all of this is already past, and will never come again.

The elderly sigh, a wave of unbearable hunger surges up, they don't even have the chance to remember the "each generation is worse than the last" curses: Now it is just a village where all crops, all livestock, and the silent land have been soaked by the flood. After the water recedes, they struggle desperately to return from a life worse than that of dogs (because it is: "Even if we die, we must die at home!"). Look, it is already: losing their homes, losing acquaintances, losing the basis for survival, the village has become just a pile of wasteland, and people can only cling to their hometown, and wait for a dreamlike destruction: to die at home.

What they still remember: is that it is "Mid-Autumn," and there is such a good moon, remembering the days of the past, remembering the scattered and deceased family members, remembering another world illuminated by the same moon, a world of lewdness and intoxicated pleasure, those "happy people!"

(How many people are hungry, so resentful and angry. So…)

The people of Lujiazhuang, dying, even hate the moon on this Mid-Autumn night. To put on a charming face in the face of disaster is simply malicious, shameless boasting, it is an insult!

It is such a season of the autumn moon, the mood of people is withering away in sorrow and hunger, just like withered leaves. The surroundings are so deathly still. In the mud, on the four walls of the houses, there is still heavy dampness, the unpleasant smell of water, the rotting smell of plants and soil. The world is so gloomy! The leaves fall softly, many unknown insect sounds ring chaotically, however, the sighs of people are silent: so subtle, so calm.

The moon, plump and full, shining from the city, seems so arrogant! It only knows to seek the joy of the nine provinces in beautiful smiling faces; and it does not have the courage to explore how many families in the world are in sorrow.

Old Tea Drinkers

— Hu Weinan

Three years ago, I was unemployed, and after being turned away everywhere, I passively went to teahouses every day to get through those long, tangled days.

The teahouse was in a narrow alley. If there wasn't a steamed bun stall at the front of the building, you might have to ask someone every day to find it. It had neither a sign like the ×× Teahouse, nor did it do a book-telling side business at night like the small teahouses next door, with a red banner advertising a specially invited ballad singer. As for how I discovered that teahouse and became a regular there for several months, I really can't remember that chance encounter.

There were only a few tea drinkers in that teahouse every day, each occupying a broken rattan chair and seeing the midday sun off to the western mountains. They were all elderly, and you could see from their eyes that they had been tempered by all kinds of environments, and now they were like old oxen abandoned in that corner. --That teahouse resembling an ancient tomb. They all sat silently, not wanting to exchange a word, for fear that it would break the air of that quiet and secluded nest. Even the few who mumbled over illustrated booklets kept their voices as soft as mosquitoes, finding a little pleasure in them with their remaining energy. Even more were those who sat all day like meditating old monks, holding dry tobacco pipes, one bag after another. So when I, such a young lad, first stepped into that teahouse, it caused them great surprise, and for several days, those almost arrow-like gazes gathered on me. But before ten days had passed, the teahouse returned to its usual calm. They didn't seem to think that the addition of a new young tea drinker would cause any trouble. Every day I brought the books and newspapers I liked to read, buried my head, drank bitter tea, and let myself suffer a little unwarranted torment.

One rainy day, only I and an old tea drinker in the next seat came to the teahouse. When the tea server, who was missing two front teeth, came to pour hot water, he sighed, "Heaven really doesn't care for the poor!" At the same time, he sat down on the side, perhaps hoping that his words would spark a conversation between us. Outside the window, it was raining heavily. If everyone continued to sit silently in the dim tea seat, it would seem like a kind of terror was about to strike. And so, the old man interjected: "The times are getting worse year by year!"

He shook his head, knocked out the embers from his tobacco pipe, and cast a pair of experienced eyes over, as if seeking my opinion. My heart was like a warehouse, full of grievances that I wanted to find an opponent to pour out. But in such a situation, I still maintained my attitude, only exchanging his gaze as if I understood his meaning.

"Young man, what do you say?"

The old man, seeing that I didn't answer, pressed me further. The tea server also raised his head, waiting for our conversation to break the dullness before the deathly silence. Thus, we started talking about everything under the sun.

The old man had once roamed all over the country alone. He wasn't like the average old person, clinging to the "old days," but he was too disappointed with everything in the "present." He hoped that we young people should be brave enough to take on this important responsibility.

"But I have knocked on so many doors of hope, and nowhere can accommodate this large group of ambitious young people!"

It seemed as if he was the opponent I had been hoping for, and I poured out the grievances that had been suppressed in my chest before him.

"But you young people always have hope," he comforted me like that.

After that, the two of us were an exception in that teahouse. Although the age difference was so great, our opinions were consistent in the discussion of every matter. I was very fortunate to have found a friend of a different generation in such a small environment.

Since finding a job and being busy with the whip of life, I could no longer go to the teahouse to meet him. It's been a full three years now. Yesterday, I happened to pass by that teahouse. I was very happy to go up and wanted to meet him, but his seat had been taken by another person, and almost all the tea drinkers were unfamiliar faces. I asked the tea server, and he said that the old man had died more than half a year ago!

On the way home, I silently recited, "You young people always have hope," and almost wanted to abandon my current job!

National Studies

Feng Mingquan's "Anthology of Classical Prose"

Mingyuan (960) 7:30 AM to 8:30 AM

Topic: Zhuangzi's "Free and Easy Wandering" (6)

I have always observed the use of poetry in the Spring and Autumn period. Poetry arose from events, not altering the events to fit the poetry. Events were gathered into the poetry, not altering the poetry to fit the events. The meaning was conveyed within the minutiae of the key points, the traces were omitted beyond the mare, the stallion, the black, and the yellow. Taking excerpts and interpreting them could lead to a divine encounter, but could not be sought through words. The petty and ignorant Confucian scholars who painstakingly explained and annotated the texts all failed at this point. Such was the skill of those who used poetry well in the Spring and Autumn period. Burned by Qin, mixed up by Han, differentiated in Qi and Lu, stirred up with apocryphal texts, confused by the Five Phases, narrowed by specialization, analyzed by the smallest weight, compared by the smallest inch. How could there be poetry left? Alas! Where can I find someone who understands the Spring and Autumn period's method of using poetry to tell them about this?

Ballad Singing

Cheng Fangzhou, Li Liansun, Mao Jiashu

Huamei (1060) 3:00 PM to 3:45 PM

Opening Chapter "Heartbroken Lyrics"

The autumn wind is lonely and falls in disorder, the cuckoo is silent and dusk is here again. I push open the moonlit window alone, the fishing lights in the river illuminate the sorrowful man. The lake water is flowing leisurely, the heart is anxious, the lonely boat is quiet and follows the riverbank. All kinds of sorrows rise from the heart, and I try to express the sorrow in my heart. People are quiet, the night is dark, the moonlight is muddy and as white as silver, Chang'e seems to know that people are frustrated, and the reunion shines on my widowed body. Recalling the past, Zhou Qing and I were in love, and we were diligent before the flowers and under the moon. She loved me, and I loved her, leaning on the lotus pond railing and singing together. I remember the two of us saying, "The sea may dry up and the rocks may rot, but our hearts will never leave." I really hoped to ride the dragon and cross the phoenix to reach Wushan, to be inseparable in life and death, but I didn't expect a violent wind to rise from the ground, blowing out the wedding candles and overturning the flower vows. And now, the fragrance has disappeared and the jade has fallen, and you have gone, Qing, and who can I tell my full of sorrow to? Fortunately, I have only tears in my eyes all year round, and I have grown thin, with a life as insignificant as my body. It is Wu Qiong's merciless emotion. Why did she especially envy her treasure hairpin skirt? I cry out, "Heaven! Heaven! Heaven! Since you gave birth to people, why give birth to hatred? Since you gave birth to hatred, why give birth to people?" Is it not that the heavenly father intentionally invades people? Is it not that five hundred years of debt have been settled in this life? Is it not that she dislikes me for being infatuated and thin, or is it not that she loves Huangpi herself and is quiet? I only wish to end the turbid world, and be alone to accompany Qing Qing. Tonight, when will I see you when I cry? The loess will bury the beautiful body for a long time. My intestines turn a few times and break inch by inch, my tearful eyes look at the jade woman's grave again, and I sincerely bow and tell my feelings, and when I look back, I see the sun rising in the east, but I hear the cuckoo singing sadly.
