Movie News

Silver Jottings

— Zhi Er

Some people say that Xu Lai is a "good person," and at first I always couldn't believe it. Recently, I saw her conversation with people in a certain newspaper, saying: "I seem to have had a dream. Those who praised me praised me up to the thirty-third heaven; those who suppressed me suppressed me into the eighteenth level of hell, but I was confused and didn't feel anything."

So, I believe that the saying that Xu Lai is a "good person" is not false.

Although Xu Lai is said to be a "good person," she is not enough to be called a "standard good person," because although she is "confused and doesn't feel anything," she still knows about being praised up to the thirty-third heaven and being suppressed into the eighteenth level of hell.

If Xu Lai is a "good person," then Diao Gongbanhua, who is called a "photo star," should also be called a "good person," or at least, should be called half a good person.

On the day "Big Family" was screened, because there were stars singing on stage, the tickets were sold out before 1:00 PM.

Alas, the value of stars.

Casual Talk About "Big Family"

"Big Family" was released on the evening of the 5th, and the tickets for the 6th were sold out, breaking the new record for box office sales in the film market this year.

In "Big Family," there are all kinds of monsters and gods, strange and bizarre things. Brothers suspect each other, sisters-in-law are jealous of each other, and the film fully portrays the various aspects of feudal society.

When the female stars took the stage, the audience cheered like thunder. When they started singing, there was silence. The singing programs included Hu Die's "Night Fragrance," Xu Lai's "The First Remember," Ye Qiuxin's "Falling Flowers and Flowing Water," Zhu Qiuhen's "Enjoying the Moment," and Gu Lanjun's "Coming Down from Qiong Lou," etc.

After the public screening of "Big Family," Wang Xianzai's "bad egg" character will surely become a "good egg," because when the scene of Wang Xianzai being deceived was shown on the screen, most of the audience had already let out sighs.

The roles of the thirty or so main actors are all developed equally. With this alone, the director has put in a lot of effort.

In the ending of "Big Family," the eldest, the second, and the third all died unnatural deaths. In front of the family hall, three memorial tablets were hung together, which was extremely tragic, and the audience shed tears of sympathy.

Old Gao and Xiao Gao are a happy couple here. Xiao Gao's control of Old Gao is no less than that of the "female hero" in the "Daughter's Classic," and she certainly does not lose Xiao Gao's true colors.

Jincheng Opens "Four Sisters"

"Four Sisters" is the latest joint production by the Liang sisters from Lianhua. The Liang sisters put a lot of effort into the film, each playing a different personality, all of which were just right, lifelike, and everyone had a role to play, each showing their skills, which was very lively. The plot was also extremely tragic and stubborn, telling the story of the life of a family of four sisters. The eldest sister was filial and obedient and sold her virginity to save her father. The second sister was weak-willed and was deceived by others because she admired prosperity, and finally repented. The third sister was infatuated, and the fourth sister was lively and innocent. There is a song in the film sung by the four Liang sisters together, which was created by Ren Guang and An E, the authors of "Fisherman's Song." The lyrics and melody are beautiful and intoxicating to listen to. The film will be publicly screened at the Jincheng Grand Theater starting today.

The Four Sisters in Lianhua's New Film "Four Sisters"

— Jincheng Ying

Oriental Theater Troupe Seeks Members

Mr. Ren Pengnian, the manager of Yueming Film Company, believes that the rise of the drama movement has a great impact on sound films. In order to cultivate new drama talents for the production of large-scale sound films, he has specially hired drama directors Ding Wanlai and Jinshan to organize the Oriental Theater Troupe, which was officially established on September 1st. The troupe is now openly recruiting members and does not charge registration fees or any other fees. The troupe will provide food and lodging and has hired a dozen experts to set up lectures. Anyone who has received secondary education or above and is in good health can apply. The application period ends on the 20th. Within the period, you can send an application form, resume, and a full-length and half-length photo to the troupe. A detailed reply will be sent. A prospectus is also available and will be sent upon request. The address is Yueming Film Company, No. 855, Bottom of Haige Road, Xiafei Road.
